# CLAUDE.md — Decision Intel

## What This Project Is

Decision Intel is a decision intelligence platform for corporate strategy teams. Users upload strategic memos, board decks, and market-entry recommendations and get a 60-second audit that scores cognitive biases, predicts steering-committee objections, and adds every decision to a living Decision Knowledge Graph that compounds over time.

**ICP — RATIFIED 2026-05-04 in GTM Plan v3.5 (canonical at [docs/gtm-plan-v3-5-2026-05-04.md](docs/gtm-plan-v3-5-2026-05-04.md); supersedes v3.4 DRAFT entirely + v3.3 selectively on wedge motion / sequencing / regulatory-tailwind timing / graduation rules; v3.3 honesty repairs all carry forward unchanged).** v3.5 narrows the Phase 1 wedge to FOUR buyer-class-continuous personas + Vohra ≥40% HXC PMF graduation gate + Outcome Gate auto-enforced on `phase1HxcEligible=true` users. 5 cross-source locks: (1) £249 wedge survives but ONLY 4 personas MARKETED (cold-context narrowing); non-wedge sign-ups get full platform access + generic overview, cohort-tagged `phase1HxcEligible=false` (Vohra-integrity, NOT an access wall — access ≠ cohort; see the 2026-05-19 amendment in the WelcomeModal lock); (2) GC + regulatory tailwinds reserved for Phase 4 (NOT Phase 1 marketing lead); (3) Bias Genome / Brier moat accumulates via Sankore engineered loops, NOT self-serve volume; (4) Linear-style rigid schema, NOT Notion-style flexibility; (5) Sankore £1,999/mo founding-pilot rate (NOT £4,999). DPR-leads-narrative reframe is SEQUENCED — top-of-funnel keeps internal-critique to fire JOLT/Brinkmanship; mid-funnel onward pivots to cover-frame ("we generate the audit-committee-ready evidence record your reasoning has to defend"). The H1 ("Decision Intel is the reasoning audit platform") stays untouched. v3.5 wedge / bridge / ceiling sequencing detailed below. The legacy v3.2 ICP framing below is still loaded by `${ICP_BLOCK}` for warm-context surfaces; v3.5 sign-up gating is the ENFORCED narrowing on cold-context.

**GTM Phase 1 wedge (months 1-6, NOW): Individual buyers @ £249/mo on FOUR buyer-class-continuous personas** — UK + US. Sign-up persona gating (shipped 2026-05-04) restricts the marketed wedge to: (a) **Fractional CSOs** running 3-5 client engagements with regular memo flow, (b) **Heads of Corporate Development / M&A at $50M-$500M revenue scale-ups** paying personally pre-team-budget, (c) **GPs / principals at smaller funds (£5M-£100M AUM)** with active deal flow OR LP-governance pressure, (d) **PE-backed mid-market founders / CEOs** with personal-decisive budget. "Other" / non-wedge sign-ups get **FULL platform access with the generic reasoning-audit overview** — the persona narrowing is cold-context MARKETING, not an access wall (warm / referral traffic must never be turned away); they are tagged `phase1HxcEligible=false` so they are EXCLUDED from the Vohra HXC graduation-gate cohort (access ≠ cohort — preserves the ≥40%-HXC signal integrity). The four personas above are the HXC cohort the Vohra survey filters to. (Access-policy amended 2026-05-19 — full reconciliation + rationale in the WelcomeModal v3.5 lock.) **Phase 1 graduation gate (locked v3.5, founder-ratified 2026-05-04): 8-12 paid Individuals retained 90+ days by month 6 (15-25 stretch)** AND **Vohra "very disappointed" ≥40% on HXC cohort** with N≥5. **Phase 1 kill criterion: <5 paid by month 4 OR Vohra <30% HXC by month 4 = halt scaling, run product-discovery sprint with somewhat-disappointed + not-disappointed cohorts. NEVER push harder on the same motion when the early-warning signal is red.** Phase 1 acquisition mix: 5-10 personalised LinkedIn DMs/week to the 4 personas (script: lead with a specific bias from one of the 143 cases that matches their industry, offer a free 60-second audit on their next memo) + 2 London events/month maximum (Strategy World London June 9-10 BAFTA = highest-signal CSO event; AI in Business Conference May 14 Prospero House = high-signal for fractional CSOs / mid-market Heads of Strategic Planning; Responsible AI Conference June 23; Momentum AI June 29-30; AI Summit London June 10-11 = lower signal-per-conversation but high volume). NO cold outbound at scale. NO advisor-network warm intros yet (those activate Phase 3). Outcome Gate auto-enforced on phase1HxcEligible=true users from day one in [/api/analyze/stream](src/app/api/analyze/stream/route.ts) (closes the policy/implementation gap CLAUDE.md previously had).

**Phase 2 bridge (months 6-12):** Sankore (London office, summer 2026 in-person 12-week design-partner engagement) — target first reference-grade pilot, in active scoping (per v3.3 §0 honesty repair #3, NOT "confirmed" until a Design Foundation MoU signs). Locked at **£1,999/mo founding-pilot rate** (NOT £4,999/mo — the Gemini PMF report's £4,999 conversion target was overruled in v3.5 cross-source synthesis because it would force cold prospects to pay MORE than the deeply-nurtured design partner; £4,999/mo is the post-Sankore Phase 3 mid-market wedge price). Plus 1-2 Individual graduates converted to differentiated pilots. £20-25K founding-pilot bundle option for 12-month commitment with optional equity-warrant + outcome-share clause. Phase 2 deliverables: ≥3 anonymised reference-grade DPR specimens + ≥5 mid-market warm intros queued for Phase 3 + per-organisation Brier-scored outcome calibration loops (the Bias Genome moat-accumulation factory) + validated team-tier feature set built FROM Sankore + Phase 1 user feedback (NOT speculatively). **Mr. Reiner / Mr. Gabe networks activate at Phase 3, NOT Phase 2 — burning them at zero-evidence is the v3.5 single most likely failure mode (Premature Enterprise Escalation).**

**Sankore engagement deepening (locked 2026-05-21 — partnership, not pilot).** First TT meeting is value-show + listen + see what happens, NOT commercial. The £1,999/mo founding-pilot rate above stays as a fallback shape, but the founder-preferred frame is a **12-week in-person embed at Sankore's newly opened London office where the trade is custom internal product in exchange for reference + access + network + retroactive calibration** — bigger and structurally different from a £1,999/mo pilot. The trade is laid out in full in the Founder Hub Sankore brief (PartnershipShape · TtMeetingPrep · LongitudinalGoals · FiveAdaptations panels). What Sankore gets: free custom-built internal decision-intelligence platform across 6+ business lines for 12+ months · a co-branded "Sankore Decision Standard" methodology · founder physically embedded · optional equity-warrant participation · optional Ligare integration roadmap. What the founder gets: access to the 14-year decision archive · embedded use across 6 business lines · **retroactive Bias Genome seed** (run DI against 30-50 closed Sankore decisions with known outcomes — the single highest-leverage moat-building move, compresses 12 months of forward calibration into 12 weeks of retroactive work) · founder-level relationship with TT · network access to her board (6-7 board-level executives at Alithia, Mines, Carbon, Cardinal Stone, Standard Chartered) · Pan-African regulatory ground-truth validation · the brand of being Sankore-embedded. **The first meeting rule (load-bearing): do NOT pitch the £249 individual tier, do NOT pitch the £1,999/mo founding-pilot rate, do NOT ask for money. If she offers, take it. The relationship + embedded access is worth 100× any monthly line item over 12 months.** Reverse the dynamic — the founder is offering 12 weeks of work at his own expense building something custom; Sankore is evaluating whether he is worth the desk space + the access. The ask is implicit; the offer is explicit.

**Revenue ceiling (12-24+ months out):** Fortune 500 corporate strategy + corp dev M&A teams @ £50K-150K ACV — **UK + US primary**. Heads of Corporate Development at FTSE 250 / S&P 500 running cross-border acquisitions; Chief Strategy Officers owning the strategic-acquisition memo workflow; audit committee + GC procurement as gate-signers. Cross-border M&A leaders specifically — where the 19-framework regulatory map (Pan-African / EM coverage: NDPR / CBN / WAEMU / PoPIA / SARB / ISA Nigeria 2007) becomes a live moat layer Cloverpop and IBM watsonx.governance don't carry.

**Pan-African / EM coverage — clarified positioning (v3.2 copy fix):** Pan-African / EM regulatory coverage is the **cross-border M&A differentiator** for the F500 ceiling buyer — a moat layer carried in the product (Dangote DPR specimen + 19-framework registry) and surfaced on `/security` + `/about`. It is NOT abandoned. What changed in v3.1 → v3.2: Pan-African / EM-focused funds are no longer the GTM wedge (that role is now individual buyers + Sankore as design partner). The moat artefact is preserved structurally; only the buyer motion shifted. A careful reader should not be able to misread this as "African coverage dropped." It is "African coverage as differentiator, not as wedge."

**Why this differs from the 2026-04-26 lock:** the prior lock had Pan-African / EM-focused funds as the GTM wedge based on a single Mr. Reiner advisor quote about word-of-mouth viral expansion. The 2026-04-30 stress-test against the founder's actual constraints (16-year-old solo founder, no warm intros to F500 corp dev today, needs first paying customer in 6 months and seed in 12-24) surfaced that procurement-cycle / reference-dependency / Sankore-strategic-incoherence concerns made the fund-wedge structurally weak. The corrected sequencing: individual UK + US buyers (frictionless wedge) → Sankore design partner bridge (warm-intro accessible, reference-producing) → F500 corp dev M&A ceiling (where the cross-border regulatory moat lives). Sankore stays as the first design partner — the strategic value is fund operational insight + reference production, not fund-buyer-budget.

**The wedge generates the cashflow + word-of-mouth that funds the bridge. The bridge generates the published references that unlock the ceiling.** Do NOT chase enterprise procurement before the graduation rule fires.

**Avoid (v3.2):** (a) Boutique sell-side M&A advisors — no software budget, relationship-driven, sceptical. (b) Generic small VC funds with no Africa/EM exposure — no procurement need, AUM-per-decision too small, relationship-driven without the capital-allocation pressure that makes the audit valuable. (c) US-only Fortune 500 with zero international M&A exposure — Cloverpop + IBM watsonx will out-bundle us in their backyard; pick fights where the cross-border regulatory moat matters.

**Connection-leverage motion (v3.2 lock):** zero warm intros to F500 corp dev today, but two connections bracket the world we need. **Mr. Reiner** (Wiz advisor → US enterprise SaaS / cybersecurity / governance acquirers): primary referral ask for 3-5 US-side warm intros to people who'd give a 20-min audit on a real memo. **Mr. Gabe** (Gabriel Osamor, CEO of Megasuto → UK investor-side network, met Apr 23 2026): primary referral ask for 3-5 UK-side warm intros via his investor clients' portfolio CSOs / corp dev heads. Discipline: every warm intro = 20-min audit on a real memo, NOT a sales pitch (the artefact does the persuasion). 4-line follow-up to introducer after every intro. Track in Founder Hub Outreach Hub. Pattern-match across 10+ before declaring the motion working.

**Sharran 1-1-1 framework (locked v3.2):** ONE traffic source (LinkedIn + warm intros), ONE conversion mechanism (20-minute audit on a real strategic memo, no slide deck), ONE delivery model (self-serve sign-up + Individual £249/mo subscription). Layered above the rest of the plan, never beneath it. Cap events at 2/month maximum to protect the 1-1-1 traffic-source discipline.

**Retroactive post-mortem cold-open + logo-minting motion (locked 2026-06-05, SF-advisor-validated).** An outside advisor independently reconstructed the v3.5 wedge + the Retroactive Audit Mode and sharpened the cold ASK three ways the toolkit didn't yet LEAD with: (1) **lead with the retro, not the forward audit** — for the deal-team wedge personas (mid-market corp dev / smaller-fund GP / PE-backed founder) the cold-open is "let me run it over a deal you've ALREADY closed," not "audit your next memo." Forensic, not predictive: you're not asking them to bet on you, only to read the past — which sidesteps the two things killing a pre-revenue solo founder (no track record + no data; the retro IS the data). Fractional CSOs keep the forward "next client memo" lead (genuinely their workflow). (2) **PAIR it** — "one you feel good about AND one that went sideways": the good deal is ego-safe, the bad one is where the value detonates. (3) **The retro is the LOGO-MINTING engine, not a conversion move** — they keep the output, you keep a case study + a real logo + the closed-outcome data that seeds the Bias Genome moat; five of these = a deck that sells itself + the wedge→bridge reference-generation engine. **Boutiques reconciliation:** the advisor named "boutique M&A advisory firms"; ICP_AVOID excludes boutique sell-side advisors as a PAID wedge (no software budget) — both hold, because the retro ask is FREE, so boutiques are a strong FREE reference/logo channel (one decision-maker, fast yes). Mint logos there, not revenue; don't let the advisor's line silently override the locked paid-wedge avoid. **SSOT:** `RETRO_POSTMORTEM_COLD_OPEN` in [icp.ts](src/lib/constants/icp.ts) (wired into `buildIcpPromptBlock()` so chat coaches it); the 3 deal-team `DM_TEMPLATES` openers in [event-prep.ts](src/lib/data/event-prep.ts) now lead with the retro; the `post_close_surprise` trigger in [discovery-pitch-toolkit.ts](src/lib/data/discovery-pitch-toolkit.ts) carries the paired-framing + logo reframe. The public [/demo](src/app/demo/page.tsx) hero now LEADS with the closed-deal retro frame ("Paste a strategic memo, closed or upcoming … run it on a deal you've already closed and see what the committee missed; the WeWork S-1 below is the same engine, in hindsight") + the placeholder + proof-label ("a closed deal we already audited") mirror it, so the landing experience a cold-DM prospect lands on matches the cold-open they were sold (the 2026-06-05 surface-audit found this was the ONE framing-gap; everything else — error handling, the Retroactive Audit Mode wizard, entry points, BAFTA leave-behinds — audited clean). Forward-looking rule: edit `RETRO_POSTMORTEM_COLD_OPEN` in icp.ts only; the DM openers + discovery trigger + chat + the /demo hero all derive from / mirror it — do NOT revert the /demo hero to forward-only "audit your next memo" framing.

**Decision system of record · positioning extension (locked v3.2):** Decision Intel is the system of record for DECISIONS specifically — not slides, not customer interviews, not competitive analysis, not the company knowledge base. Just the decisions + their outcomes + the reasoning trail. Stay narrow: the narrowness is the moat. The CSO value-prop extension follows: _"All your deals and their outcomes live in Decision Intel. Decision history survives team transitions. Audit-committee Q&A pulls up reasoning in 60 seconds. Future decisions get sharper because the platform learns YOUR specific bias patterns."_ Never drift into "your full knowledge base" framing — that cedes territory to Notion / Confluence / Drive and dilutes the decision-specific moat. **"company knowledge base" added to banned-vocabulary list 2026-04-30** for this exact discipline reason.

**Outcome Gate enforced on Individual tier (v3.2 lock — supersedes the v3.1 pulse-survey softening that was Cloverpop's data-advantage trap):** Outcome Gate enforcement stays ON for Individual tier from day one. Friction is engineered out through automation (auto-detection via Drive / Slack / email, one-click confirm-or-override drafts via PATCH `/api/outcomes/draft`, outcome-gated feature unlocks for Decision DNA / Bias Genome contribution / cross-org cohort comparison) plus a "why this matters" inline rationale at every Outcome Gate moment — anchored in Klein & Mitchell 1995 (prospective hindsight produces 25-30% more failure-cause insights), the 143-case calibration baseline, and per-org Brier-scored recalibration. **The discipline: Outcome Gate becomes the unlock mechanism, not the tax.** Every closed outcome compounds the platform's value to the user specifically AND compounds the data moat that makes a $50-150M strategic acquisition defensible (vs. Cloverpop's data-advantage attack vector). Pulse-survey approach REJECTED — it was identified as the path to a £300K/yr lifestyle utility, not the data asset required for the $30M+ founder cash exit.

**Agentic-shift defensive acceleration (v3.2 lock):** the audit-layer-for-agents pivot evaluation moved from "Q3 2026 reserve" → 30-day parallel investigation in May-June 2026. Sample 10 prospects via warm intros with the discovery question _"How are your strategic acquisition memos and IC decks being authored today — fully human, AI-assisted, or agent-generated?"_ Three forward paths: memos still human-authored → wedge motion holds; memos heavily AI-assisted → wedge motion holds, positioning sharpens; memos agent-generated → audit motion shifts to auditing agent prompts + outputs (same R²F + DPR architecture, different input shape). One-page memo drafted by end of June 2026 documents the prospect-level evidence. The founder finds out NOW, not in October.

**$30M+ founder cash exit target (locked v3.2, dual-track funding update 2026-05-03):** Two tracks now active — see GTM v3.3 §10 for the full lock.

- **Primary track (unchanged) — bootstrap-to-seed.** Bootstrap-leaning + ONE strategic seed round Q4 2026 / Q1 2027 at £1.5-2.5M on £8-15M post-money (founder dilution 12-20%). Bootstrap to £3-8M ARR over 3-5 years post-seed. Strategic acquisition exit at 8-12× ARR multiple = £30-95M EV. Likely acquirers: LRQA, IBM watsonx.governance arm, Big-4 governance practice, or a strategic AI-governance player TBD. Founder retains 60-78% post-seed → personal cash $25-70M, comfortably clearing the $30M floor. **5 candidate seed funds** (paths to be activated, NOT priority order): Conviction Partners (Sarah Guo) · Cyberstarts (Gili Raanan) · Elad Gil (solo angel) · Index Ventures (Mark Goldberg / Hannah Seal UK) · Neo (Ali Partovi). When to raise (per Mr. Gabe rule): customers before investors — lock the seed conversation only after 5+ paid Individual customers + 1+ Design Foundation pilot signed + 1+ verifiable referral via DPR + 50+ qualified waitlist contacts.

- **Secondary track (newly added 2026-05-03) — opportunistic pre-seed.** $200K post-money SAFE at ~10% post-money cap ($2M) — _deck currently shows $1.5M post-money / ~13% dilution; founder's verbal terms are 10%; ALIGN BEFORE SENDING the deck to any partner_. Purpose is primarily NETWORK ACCESS through the VC's portfolio relationships, not the capital — the VC partner's portfolio CSO / corp-dev relationships compress time-to-first-customer + time-to-Sankore-pilot, which improves the seed round's traction story. In active talks with one pre-investment-fund VC partner (founder doesn't want to name; keep generic on shipped surfaces per the no-named-prospects rule). 12-month runway use of funds: 40% founder-led GTM + pilots ($80K), 25% engineering contractors ($50K), 20% SOC 2 Type I issuance + Type II observation start + AI Verify alignment ($40K), 15% reference-grade DPR specimens ($30K). Pre-seed close milestones: 5+ paying Individuals ($15K ARR) + 1+ Design Foundation pilot + 1+ verifiable DPR referral + **SOC 2 Type I issued (Q4 2026 target) with Type II observation window underway** + vendor continuity plan documented + seed conversation opens 12-15 months out. **Calendar reconciliation 2026-05-05:** the prior milestone language said "SOC 2 Type II certified" within a 12-month runway, which is unachievable — Type II requires a 6-12 month observation period AFTER Type I issuance. The corrected milestone language ("Type I issued + Type II observation underway") matches the actual SOC2_RECEIPTS posture in [trust-copy.ts](src/lib/constants/trust-copy.ts) (Type I targeted Q4 2026, Type II window opens immediately after). When a partner asks during diligence "is the SOC 2 milestone realistic?", the answer is yes because the language now aligns with the timeline. If the runway extends past 18 months, this milestone can flip to "Type II issued" without further reconciliation.

**How the two tracks interact:** pre-seed at $200K / 10% does NOT replace the seed round — it complements it. Founder dilution math: $200K at 10% pre-seed + ~$2M at 15% seed = ~25% by Series A; founder still owns ~60% post-Series-A on the $30M+ cash exit math. The Mr. Gabe customers-before-investors rule still applies to the SEED — the pre-seed is a network play, not a pre-customer hypothesis lock. Reject the pre-seed if (a) terms drift from founder-friendly (>10% / pushes for board seat / blocking rights at $200K is too small to warrant), (b) the partner's network access turns out to be performative not actual, (c) the partner's diligence implies governance overhead that slows the wedge motion.

**Reference source-of-truth (now v3.5, RATIFIED 2026-05-04):** canonical plan is [docs/gtm-plan-v3-5-2026-05-04.md](docs/gtm-plan-v3-5-2026-05-04.md). Mirror file lives in master KB notebook `809f5104-c36f-4360-9e20-ef79c752a8cd`. When this lock changes, update CLAUDE.md + `src/lib/constants/icp.ts` + the master KB source + `src/lib/data/discovery-pitch-toolkit.ts` (if motion changes) in the same commit so chat coaching, founder-facing copy, and synthesis layer stay in lockstep.

**Current phase: Refinement & consolidation.** The product has 200+ components and 70+ API routes — more features than most Series A companies. The priority is polishing the core flow (upload → analyze → review → track outcomes) to attract pilot users and raise pre/seed funding. Push back on scope creep. If a change doesn't make the first 60 seconds of a demo better, it probably shouldn't be the priority.

**Anti-scope-creep vs boil-the-ocean — resolution rule (locked 2026-04-27).** This file's "push back on scope creep" instruction and the user-memory `feedback-boil-the-ocean` ("do the whole thing right on non-trivial builds; no workarounds, no dangling threads") both apply. The decision rule when they collide: **was the work explicitly approved as planned/Tier-N execution?** If yes (founder said "proceed with Tier 1," "ship the deep version," "implement this list," etc.) — boil-the-ocean wins. Default to the category-grade enterprise version of every approved item; never the lean cut. If the work is an unsolicited polish opportunity, a side-quest discovered mid-task, or an "I noticed we could also…" — anti-scope-creep wins; flag it, don't ship it. Test for category-grade-on-planned-work: before declaring done, sit in the buyer's seat (CSO / fund partner / GC / IC reviewer) and answer (a) "what's the next question I'd ask on this surface?" (b) "what action would I take from here?" (c) "what claim looks weak from a procurement reader's perspective?" If any of those reveal a gap, deepen before shipping. Time estimates on planned work are depth signals ("this much depth is the target"), NOT time budgets ("come in under this if you can").

**Velocity & Scope Discipline — session-level estimation (locked 2026-05-09 after 7 commits in one afternoon collapsed a 6-month roadmap).** A calibration anchor for every future planning conversation:

The M&A roadmap was originally written with month-anchored phases — P1 Months 1-3, P2 Months 4-6, P3 Months 7-9, Backlog post-acqui-hire. **Actual elapsed time for P1 + P2's load-bearing portion + 5 adjacent ships: one afternoon.** Specifically (2026-05-09):

1. `cfdffdbc` — P1: 13 named toxic combinations + 9 M&A document subtypes + cascade across BIAS_DETECTIVE_PROMPT + Education Room + chat + CLAUDE.md
2. `15faa00` — Onboarding `ma` cascade: 3 new sample bundles + 4-stop tour + 4-surface empty states
3. `f39eea7` — Marketing data cascade across 6 surfaces + first 7 anchor cases retro-tagged
4. `07b7c5f` — Deeper 7-case retro-tagging (14 total) + bias-count drift fix + count-discipline lockstep
5. `2c7524e` — `/bias-genome` M&A Pattern Coverage section + `/how-it-works` deal-stage overlays Section 4b
6. `8719c09` — WelcomeModal `VALUE_PROPS_BY_ROLE` + tour 3→4 stops + dashboard subtitle + first-run pitch
7. `9eddb2c` — P2 synergy parser (1050 LOC structured spreadsheet parsing + per-claim defensibility scoring + 21 vitest tests + critical upload-validation bug fix)

The pre-AI-pair-programming velocity model is dead. Forward-looking rules:

(1) **Anchor estimates to sessions, not months.** When proposing scope, the right question is "ships in N sessions" not "fits in Q3 2026." A roadmap item that says "Months 7-9" probably ships in 1-2 sessions when picked up.

(2) **Default to the deeper version when the founder says proceed.** The boil-the-ocean rule is stronger than initially calibrated. When the founder approves planned/Tier-N work, ship the full cascade — every surface, every test, every CLAUDE.md update — not the lean cut. The afternoon ship cluster above proves the cascade is absorbable in one go.

(3) **The cascade discipline scales.** A 10-surface lockstep ship (4 internal pipeline + 6 marketing data structures + ≥1 case-tagging) is the M&A example; the same shape applies to bias taxonomy (10+ surfaces) + onboarding (5 surfaces per role) + DPR vocabulary (16+ surfaces). When a lock changes, propagate the FULL cascade in the same commit — the gates catch nothing if 1 of 10 surfaces drifts, but the buyer sees the gap immediately.

(4) **Don't pre-shrink the proposal.** When laying out options for the founder's choice, propose the depth that's actually shippable in the session, not the lean version anchored to a stale velocity model. If the founder wants narrower, they'll say. Pre-shrinking burns the founder's time and forces a re-prompt to expand.

(5) **Quarter-anchored language in roadmap docs is stale convention, not real scheduling.** When you read "Months 4-6, during Sankore window" in CLAUDE.md, treat it as a phase ordering signal (P2 follows P1; do P1 first), not a literal calendar estimate.

(6) **Calibration check before declaring scope:** if the proposed scope feels like it can ship in this session AND the founder asked for thorough work, the scope is too small — deepen until it's session-bounded but cascade-complete.

(7) **Surface hard-layer improvements proactively (locked 2026-05-09 evening).** When auditing a multi-commit ship, scan for changes in the pipeline (`src/lib/agents/`), DQI scoring (`src/lib/scoring/`), graph state shape (`src/lib/agents/graph.ts`), or Prisma schema that would meaningfully deepen the architecture — and surface them to the founder with rationale + cost + risk before declaring the ship complete. Default-skipping these layers is pre-shrinking. The "Modifying the analysis pipeline" rule's true intent is "don't ship silently," not "don't propose." Every ship cycle ends with a brief self-audit: "what did I deliberately skip touching the hard layers, and was that the right call?" Items where the answer is "no" get surfaced as a brief decision matrix to the founder.

This rule was added because pre-shrinking suboptimised the founder's leverage. The founder pays per session; the unit economics favour depth over caution. When in doubt, ship the deep version — and when in doubt about whether to TOUCH the hard layers, surface the proposal rather than silently skip.

## One-liner (RE-LOCKED 2026-05-04 — CATEGORY-CLAIM PIVOT)

**Primary H1 (landing + pitch-deck slide 1 + LinkedIn headline):**

> **Decision Intel is the reasoning audit platform.**

**Contrast sub-head (use as second sentence on landing + pitch deck):**

> **Most tools audit your data. We audit your reasoning — and catch the fatal blind spots in strategic memos before the committee does.**

**Asymmetric-tail body (justification for running the audit on every memo, not just the suspicious ones):**

> **Most strategic memos pass cleanly. The ones that don't are the ones that destroy value. You can't tell the catastrophic memo from the clean memo without auditing both — which is why you run the audit on every memo, not just the suspicious ones.**

**Secondary H1 (cold investor + regulatory-tailwind contexts only):**

> **The reasoning audit platform the Fortune 500 needs before EU AI Act enforcement begins August 2026.**

**Rules:**

- **"The reasoning audit platform"** is the protected category noun. Treat like R²F / DPR / DQI — never substitute synonyms ("reasoning analyser", "reasoning checker", "decision audit platform") in shipped surfaces. The category becomes ownable through CONSISTENT REPETITION; one-off paraphrases dilute the claim. Only allowed deviation: drop "platform" → "the reasoning audit" for cold contexts (LinkedIn DM character limits, conference 1-line introductions) where SaaS-platform vocabulary feels heavy.
- **The category-claim test (James Pursey 15-second test):** a stranger hears the H1 and resolves all three terms (software → audits → human thinking) immediately without lookup. The new claim passes; the prior "native reasoning layer for every high-stakes call" failed because both "reasoning layer" and "high-stakes call" required the reader to pause and define abstract terms before the sentence completed.
- **The category-claim move ("THE platform" not "A platform")** asserts category ownership the way "Stripe is the payments infrastructure for the internet" does. The category — _reasoning-audit-platform_ — does not exist as a Gartner segment, which means it's ours by usage. The claim differentiates cleanly from BI tools (audit data) and model-risk-management tools (audit algorithms) by baking the human-reasoning differentiator into the noun itself.
- **The contrast sub-head** does the differentiator work the H1 alone can't carry. Use as the second sentence on the landing page and pitch deck slide 1.
- **The asymmetric-tail body** captures the "very much might not but when it does, it's a big thing" insight that justifies running the audit on EVERY memo. Goes immediately below the contrast sub-head; never in the H1 itself.
- **Do NOT** use "collaborative," "collaborator," "medium," or "protect outcomes" framings. **Banned drift targets** (per `BANNED_VOCABULARY` in `icp.ts`): `decision intelligence platform` (Gartner-crowded), `decision hygiene` (Kahneman's term), `boardroom strategic decision` (audience-narrowing), `company knowledge base` (dilutes the decision-specific moat), `AI decision tool` (generic SaaS tell), `AI-powered decision platform` (AI-powered prefix is a generic SaaS tell), **`native reasoning layer`** (deprecated 2026-05-04 — failed Pursey 15-second test), **`bad strategic decisions`** (deprecated 2026-05-08 — accusatory toward elite buyers), and **`unaudited decisions`** alone without "reasoning" (deprecated 2026-05-08 — drops the IP differentiator).
- "Reasoning layer" stays valid in long-form technical writing where the architectural metaphor is load-bearing (e.g., explaining how DI sits between data infrastructure and decision execution), but it is NEVER the H1 or first impression. The category is "the reasoning audit platform"; "reasoning layer" is now legacy supporting vocabulary.
- "Protected revenue" framing (per the 2026-04-27 lock) stays valid as a body-copy explainer but the H1 leads with the category claim, not the protected-revenue framing. The two layer cleanly: H1 = category, body = protected revenue.

## Pain Framing (RE-LOCKED 2026-05-08 — NotebookLM-VERIFIED PIVOT FROM "BAD STRATEGIC DECISIONS")

**Canonical pain phrase** (slide 2 of pitch deck, landing-page problem statement, cold outreach openers, anywhere we name the problem):

> **Capital eroded by unaudited reasoning in strategic decisions.**

**Money-line philosophical claim** (rehearsable, quotable, pitch-deck-ready — anchored in Mercier & Sperber argumentative theory + Kahneman & Klein 2009 conditions for trustworthy intuition):

> **Reasoning is never objectively sound; it is either audited or unaudited.**

**Source-of-truth in code:** `POSITIONING_PAIN_FRAMING` + `POSITIONING_PAIN_PHILOSOPHICAL_CLAIM` + `COMPETITIVE_DEFENSIVE_LINES` exports in [src/lib/constants/icp.ts](src/lib/constants/icp.ts). When the pain framing changes, edit `icp.ts` first; every consumer reads by import.

**Why "unaudited reasoning" beats "bad / flawed reasoning":** elite decision-makers (CSO, M&A head, GP, PE-backed founder) view their intuition as their proprietary edge and reject framing that says their reasoning is broken. Per the master-KB synthesis: "telling a Fortune 500 CSO that their reasoning is FLAWED triggers immediate ego threat and destroys the sale." "Unaudited" names a missing process, not broken thinking — ego-safe + procurement-grade.

**Why "unaudited reasoning" beats "unaudited decisions" alone:** dropping "reasoning" abandons the IP moat. Cloverpop logs decisions; IBM watsonx audits models. Both can co-opt "we audit decisions." The word **reasoning** is the legal lock — it preserves the 22-bias taxonomy + R²F + 143-case corpus + Kahneman/Klein synthesis as the differentiator no competitor carries.

**Underlying philosophical claim:** human reasoning is biologically and evolutionarily flawed by default. Capital is not destroyed because executives have cognitive biases — biases are the OS of the human mind. Capital is destroyed because organizations lack the structural friction (the audit) required to catch and neutralize bias before capital is committed.

**Competitive defensive lines** (locked alongside the pain framing 2026-05-08, use verbatim when buyer / investor names a competitor):

- **Cloverpop:** _"Cloverpop logs decisions; Decision Intel audits them."_
- **IBM watsonx.governance:** _"IBM audits the model; Decision Intel audits the human reasoning."_

These two lines are the operational follow-through to the pain framing — the pain phrase preserves "reasoning" as the IP differentiator; the defensive lines collect on that preservation when a competitor name comes up.

## AI-Native Ex-Ante-Additive Reframe (locked 2026-05-29 — NARRATION cascade, not a build; adversarial-verified against the AI-native Deep Research pass)

**Why this exists.** After seeing Wealor (YC P26) and other "true AI-native" platforms, the founder asked how DI becomes a genuinely novel AI-native platform — unifying AI-native + saves-the-user-time + the bias/noise angle + helping users build the audit in the first place (ex-ante), not just running it on a finished memo. A Gemini Deep Research report ("The Epistemic Architecture of Strategic Decision-Making") was commissioned, then pressure-tested with an 8-agent adversarial workflow that code-verified its claims against the shipped surfaces. **The diagnosis: DI is AI-powered-tool-shaped in its NARRATION (request→response: "paste a memo, get a grade"), but already AI-native in its SURFACES.** The fix is a positioning/narration reframe, NOT a product rewrite.

**What the adversarial pass concluded (the synthesis that governs this lock):**

- **~70% of the report's recommendations re-described surfaces DI already ships.** Every ex-ante / ambient surface named as "what AI-native would look like" exists: PriorsCaptureCard, the Intelligent Antagonist / Constellation Next Move, reference-class forecast, the Deal Fever pre-mortem, forced ≤90-day operational proxies (V1), ambient capture (Slack full + Drive file-body, opt-in / 500-char / 14-day / no-raw-persist), per-org Brier + cross-org Bias Genome. The gap was that the pitch led with the ex-post audit and buried the upstream work.
- **The one genuinely net-new idea = MAP (Mediating Assessments Protocol** — Kahneman / Lovallo / Sibony, _Noise_ 2021): decompose a decision into independent attributes, blind-score each on objective criteria BEFORE any holistic discussion, delay the global judgment. It is the noise-side complement to the bias-heavy R²F stack and defeats the halo/coherence cascade (DI-B-021). **UNSHIPPED** — the current noise jury is decorrelated FRAMES (analyst-skeptical / regulator-hostile / contrarian-strategist), which is framing-variance, NOT attribute-decomposition-with-blind-scoring. MAP is the **queued next R²F detector**; the engine is a founder-gated pipeline change (methodology bump 2.4.0 → 2.5.0 + held-out parity run) **deferred post-first-customer**. Speak it as roadmap, never as a current capability.
- **Report recommendations REJECTED** (do not act on these even though they're in the paper): **R2** — "ship a Word/Google-Docs co-authoring extension" — redundant (the ambient Drive path already ingests file bodies), IT-blocked at the F500/procurement buyer, and a privacy-posture violation. **R4** — "abandon the DQI score and the ex-post memo audit, pivot to a co-creation tool" — moat-suicide (the DPR is the EU AI Act Art 14 contractual artefact; the DQI is the scalar the per-org Bias Genome scores against) AND self-contradictory with the report's own R5 data-flywheel recommendation. **The discipline: ADD upstream co-creation narration, KEEP every existing surface.**

**The reframe (NARRATION ONLY — the H1 "Decision Intel is the reasoning audit platform" + the Four Moments are UNCHANGED):**

- **Lead ex-ante-additive, not ex-post-corrective.** Canonical frames live in [icp.ts](src/lib/constants/icp.ts) `POSITIONING_EX_ANTE_FRAME` ("We help you build defensible reasoning before conviction locks in — the reference class, the pre-mortem, the dissent that costs no political capital — and the audit-committee record falls out of it.") + `POSITIONING_TIME_SAVING_FRAME` ("It does the reasoning-hygiene work you skip under deadline … so the rigor is additive, not another step."). The memo audit + DPR + DQI are the procurement / defensibility BACKSTOP, not the headline.
- **Demo ordering:** lead with PriorsCapture + the Intelligent Antagonist (the upstream co-creation), then show the DPR / DQI as the backstop the record falls out into. Do NOT open the demo on "paste a memo → here's your grade."
- **NARROWNESS GUARD (load-bearing, the moat):** DI co-creates the REASONING (reference class, pre-mortem, priors, antagonist), it NEVER authors the deliverable (memo / IC packet / LP letter). `'auto-draft the memo'` and `'decision co-creation platform'` are in `BANNED_VOCABULARY` ([icp.ts](src/lib/constants/icp.ts)) — the horizontal Quantellia / Aera / Wealor trap. Narrowness is the moat; the reframe must not drift DI into a horizontal decision-authoring tool.
- **DQI "black-box / arbitrary grade" rebuttal** (shipped across pricing FAQ + Sparring + Education + founder-context): "It's not a black-box grade — here's the slider (weights are user-adjustable, the Dietvorst 2016 algorithm-aversion fix), the per-component breakdown, and the tamper-evident hash on the DPR." Reproducible weighted methodology (v2.4.0), not a verdict imposed.
- **DO-NOT-QUOTE** (confabulated Deep Research figures — same discipline as Brier 0.258 / ~90% margin): "~30h saved per deal", "+30% failure-cause identification", "55% of variance is noise". Shape conviction with them; never cite them as stats.

**Cascade shipped in this lock (NARRATION surfaces only — zero changes to `src/lib/agents/` or the DQI engine):** `icp.ts` SSOT (the two frames + `buildPositioningPromptBlock()` ex-ante narration block + BANNED_VOCABULARY + a cold-context onramp) · [founder-context.ts](src/app/api/founder-hub/founder-context.ts) chat-coaching block · Education Room (MAP flashcard in `r2f_framework` + ex-ante-narration flashcard in `founder_oneliners`) · Sparring Room (ex-ante-timing objection + DQI black-box-grade objection scenarios) · pricing FAQ (DQI-is-not-a-black-box-grade rebuttal). Research prompt + adversarial synthesis archived in [docs/research/](docs/research/).

**Forward-looking rule:** when the ex-ante frames evolve, edit `POSITIONING_EX_ANTE_FRAME` / `POSITIONING_TIME_SAVING_FRAME` in `icp.ts` only — every consumer reads via import or mirrors the SSOT. **MAP stays a roadmap exhibit until it is founder-approved as a pipeline ship** (methodology bump + held-out parity + the bias-taxonomy / noise-jury cascade); never let a surface claim MAP is live. The "produce the middle" surfaces (auto-RCF / auto-pre-mortem fired off the priors surface before the memo exists), ambient email ingestion, and the MAP engine are all DEFERRED, post-first-customer, founder-gated — they are recorded scope boundaries, not silent omissions.

**MAP roadmap exhibit + R²F synthesis line — locked 2026-05-30 (founder-approved).** Two narration ships, zero pipeline touch. (1) **MAP is now a published roadmap exhibit on `/r2f-standard`** — the R²F Detector Atlas ([R2FDetectorAtlas.tsx](src/components/marketing/r2f-standard/R2FDetectorAtlas.tsx)) gained a `status: 'shipped' | 'queued'` field + MAP as queued entry #11 (Grid2x2 icon, blind-attribute-decomposition mini-viz, amber ROADMAP chip on the card + amber "Roadmap · queued" badge + an explicit roadmap-note callout naming the methodology-bump + held-out-parity + post-first-customer gating in the detail panel). The section eyebrow + body derive the shipped/queued split from `DETECTORS.filter(...)` (`SHIPPED_COUNT`/`QUEUED_COUNT`) so it can't drift; the entry's `liveSurfaces` is empty + renders "Not yet shipped — roadmap entry". This is the "speak MAP as roadmap, never as a current capability" rule made a procurement/diligence asset without any pipeline risk. When MAP ships as a real detector, flip `status` to `'shipped'` + populate `shippedDate`/`implementationFiles`/`liveSurfaces` + drop `roadmapNote` in the same commit. (2) **`POSITIONING_SYNTHESIS_LINE` = "Don't replace intuition. Audit it."** — new canonical constant in [icp.ts](src/lib/constants/icp.ts), the four-word human-facing crystallization of `IP_MOAT_DESCRIPTION` (the Kahneman × Klein synthesis). Surfaced as the R²F-page hero lead line (under the H1, above the descriptive subtitle) + in `buildPositioningPromptBlock()` chat coaching. It is the one-line answer to "are you replacing the CSO's judgment?" — ego-safe (audits a process, never calls the thinking broken — same discipline as `POSITIONING_PAIN_FRAMING`) + IP-true ("audit" = the reasoning-audit category). **NOT the landing H1** — that stays `POSITIONING_HERO_PRIMARY`. Forward-looking: edit the line in `icp.ts` only; the R²F page + chat both read the SSOT.

**Epistemic-honesty / causality discipline — locked 2026-05-31 (GPT-pushback-validated; turns the sharpest sophisticated-buyer challenge into the moat).** A close read of the codebase (prompted by GPT's pushback, founder-endorsed) found the engine + marketing copy already correlational-careful, but the **case-study FAQPage JSON-LD** (`generateCaseStudyFaqs` in [seo.ts](src/lib/data/case-studies/seo.ts)) asked _"Which cognitive biases **caused** [Company]'s [outcome]?"_ across every case — a causal overclaim baked into the exact machine-readable layer the GEO/AEO push feeds to AI engines (they cite FAQ pairs verbatim). The fix is also the differentiator. **Canonical SSOT:** `POSITIONING_EPISTEMIC_HONESTY` in [icp.ts](src/lib/constants/icp.ts) — _"Decision Intel identifies reasoning-risk indicators correlated with poor outcomes — it does not claim to establish causation. That honesty is the procurement weapon: a CSO can defend a score that names the risk indicators a committee should pressure-test, not one that pretends to prove the cause."_ **Cascade shipped (copy/data/SSOT/lint only — zero `src/lib/agents/` or DQI-engine change):** (1) `seo.ts` FAQ#1 softened to _"were evident in"_ + a NEW explicit FAQ _"Did these cognitive biases cause [Company]'s [outcome]?"_ whose answer is the SSOT line + "whether they caused it is a question no audit can settle" — so the honest correlational answer is now what AI engines cite; (2) `icp.ts` constant + wired into `buildPositioningPromptBlock()` (3-beat rebuttal: agree → reframe to risk-indicators → close on audit-committee defensibility); (3) [scripts/lint-positioning.mjs](scripts/lint-positioning.mjs) **precise** guard `/\bwhich\s+(cognitive\s+)?biases?\s+caused\b/i` — fires on the old interrogative product-claim shape, verified SILENT on historical-analysis prose ("authority bias caused leaders to override…" in the 143-case library is legitimate documented analysis, NOT a DI product claim — deliberately not flagged); (4) public differentiator section on [/r2f-standard](<src/app/(marketing)/r2f-standard/R2FStandardClient.tsx>) — _"What the audit establishes · and what it deliberately doesn't"_ (`#epistemic-honesty`); (5) BAFTA-rehearsal trio — founder-context.ts chat-coaching block + a Sparring `objection_handler` scenario (`midmarket_corp_dev`, distinct from the false-precision + algorithm-aversion scenarios) + an Education `silent_objections` flashcard (`silent_causality_correlation`). **Forward-looking rule:** edit `POSITIONING_EPISTEMIC_HONESTY` in `icp.ts` only — every consumer reads/mirrors the SSOT. NEVER let marketing or JSON-LD copy assert a detected bias CAUSED a historical outcome (the lint guard enforces the interrogative shape; the affirmative discipline is "correlated risk indicators, not cause"). Historical-analysis prose in the case library may describe documented causation — that is analysis, not a product claim; do not "fix" it.

**Superforecasting / Tetlock calibration leg + Active Open-Mindedness — locked 2026-06-05 (narration cascade + one cited engine backfill; founder-approved "boil the oceans" after the Superforecasting synthesis).** A Superforecasting essay was mapped against the SHIPPED code (grep-before-assert — the prior session had the wrong path for the engine, `src/lib/scoring/bayesian-priors.ts` not `learning/`). Verdict: ~90% of the essay's "platform applications" already ship (reference-class forecast = outside view; the 3-frame noise jury + boardroom twin = dragonfly-eye; the forced ≤90-day operational-proxy Brier loop = granular timelines; PriorsCaptureCard belief-delta via `applyBayesianPriors` = Bayesian updating). The leverage was NARRATION, not a build: frame **Tetlock as the MEASUREMENT third leg** on top of the R²F Kahneman × Klein synthesis (R²F is NOT renamed — Tetlock is an ADDED leg), name **Active Open-Mindedness (AOM)** as the already-shipped Intelligent Antagonist (the user's prior is captured BEFORE the algorithm reveals its read; the gap is the signal), and lock the **do-not-quote honesty guardrails**. **Canonical SSOT:** `POSITIONING_CALIBRATION_LEG` + `POSITIONING_ACTIVE_OPEN_MINDEDNESS` + `SUPERFORECASTING_DO_NOT_QUOTE` in [icp.ts](src/lib/constants/icp.ts), wired into `buildPositioningPromptBlock()`. **Cascade (narration only — zero `src/lib/agents/` change):** (1) icp.ts SSOT; (2) [founder-context.ts](src/app/api/founder-hub/founder-context.ts) chat-coaching block (zero backticks — template-literal balance verified even); (3) Education Room — 3 `r2f_framework` flashcards (calibration leg, AOM, Brier-vs-DQI honesty); (4) Sparring — a `preseed_vc_associate` × `objection_handler` "calibration-claim probe" where the WIN is the RESTRAINT (drills the do-not-quote discipline under VC pressure; distinct from the 4 existing wrapper scenarios); (5) public [/r2f-standard](<src/app/(marketing)/r2f-standard/R2FStandardClient.tsx>) — a "What Brier scores, and what it doesn't" callout in the `#calibration` section (on-brand with the existing epistemic-honesty pattern, minimal em-dashes). **The one engine change** (founder-approved, separate from narration): [bayesian-priors.ts](src/lib/scoring/bayesian-priors.ts) `BIAS_BASE_RATES` covered 16 of the 22-bias taxonomy; the other 6 silently fell to `DEFAULT_BASE_RATE = 0.5` (halo_effect, gamblers_fallacy, zeigarnik_effect, paradox_of_choice, illusion_of_validity DI-B-021, inside_view_dominance DI-B-022 — the last two the most Tetlock-relevant). Backfilled with real cited base rates (Nisbett & Wilson 1977 / Tversky & Kahneman 1971 / Zeigarnik 1927 / Iyengar & Lepper 2000 conservative / Einhorn & Hogarth 1978 / Kahneman & Lovallo 1993), kept in lockstep with the `getAllBaseRates` citation map; new [bayesian-priors.test.ts](src/lib/scoring/bayesian-priors.test.ts) (11 tests) locks the taxonomy-coverage invariant so a future 23rd bias can't silently regress to 0.5. **Scope-safe**: `applyBayesianPriors` only fires when a user `DecisionPrior` exists (risk-compiler `applyBayesianAdjustment` returns unchanged otherwise, 80/20-blended), so the no-prior DQI distribution is byte-identical (held-out `dqi-distribution-check` confirms) — NO methodology bump. **Do-not-quote (locked verbatim in `SUPERFORECASTING_DO_NOT_QUOTE`):** Brier ≠ DQI (DQI grades the reasoning; Brier grades our calibration on the forecasts — never "Brier-scored DQI", a category error a sophisticated buyer catches); the GJP "23% more accurate / constructive confrontation" is a HUMAN-team result, the noise jury is "decorrelated samples, not formally independent judges" (never a "superteam"); extremizing the aggregate could DEGRADE a decorrelated-not-independent jury's calibration (it assumes diverse INDEPENDENT private information) — **DEFERRED, founder-gated, may fail a held-out parity run, NOT roadmap-confident.** That last item is the recorded boundary: it is the one Superforecasting idea I refused to ship even under "boil the oceans," because I had argued it could backfire on this architecture — boil-the-ocean means depth on the right work, not shipping a change I refuted. **Forward-looking rule:** edit the three constants in `icp.ts` only; every consumer reads/mirrors the SSOT. When a 23rd bias lands, add its base rate + citation to BOTH maps in `bayesian-priors.ts` (the coverage test enforces it). Never let a surface conflate Brier with DQI or claim the GJP human-team stat as ours.

## Paper-grounded findings + Tier plan (locked 2026-05-10 evening — second Deep Research paper)

**Source**: 2026-05-10 Deep Research paper _"Structural Failure Analysis of Decision-Quality Interventions in Corporate Development and Mergers and Acquisitions"_ (150+ sources). Anchored on Kyle Price (Roblox, NOT YouTube) verbatim quotes from M&A Science podcast — indexed in NotebookLM master KB `809f5104` as source #23 (`1322d9ac-28f...`). Mirror: [docs/paper-grounded-tier-plan-2026-05-10.md](docs/paper-grounded-tier-plan-2026-05-10.md) carries the full session-handoff plan including DQI-weight-adjustability implementation sketch + PMI strategic question.

**Four counter-intuitive findings** that demolished or sharpened parts of the existing positioning:

1. **Awareness does not reduce bias** (Boomerang Effect, Pronin et al. 2002) — educating practitioners on biases paradoxically _increases_ their overconfidence + vulnerability. **Implication**: bias-education-heavy first impressions on `/bias-genome` + `/how-it-works` are a structural liability. Reframe to _"what the audit caught"_ not _"learn the biases."_ Keep the 22-bias taxonomy as DPR-methodology IP exhibit (procurement readers want to see the framework backbone); demote it from first-impression position. NEVER delete `/bias-genome` / `/taxonomy` / Education Room — they're the IP moat. Reposition them as second-impression methodology exhibits, not first-impression marketing claims.

2. **Red teams fail to scale because they're structurally antagonistic** (Ch 2 of paper). Political/ego cost is unsustainable in high-velocity sponsor-driven environments — they degrade into performative _"list-the-risks"_ exercises. **Implication**: the _"always-on red team"_ category-claim framing fails the paper's test — we'd inherit red teams' bad properties. Sharper claim: _"the antagonist that costs you no political capital"_ + _"the audit that fires before the IC memo can hide it."_ Banned from cold-context on-ramps as of 2026-05-10: any phrasing that positions DI as a digitised red team. The DI's intelligent-antagonist pattern absorbs the political cost of dissent; the human user becomes a facilitator, not an antagonist (Ch 10 finding).

3. **The "false precision" objection is mostly ego-defense, not strategic wisdom** (Meehl 1954, Dawes 1979, Grove et al. 2000 — mechanical models outperform clinical intuition even with uniform/improper weights). Algorithm Aversion (Dietvorst, Simmons & Massey 2015 _J. Exp. Psychol. General_, doi:10.1037/xge0000033) names the failure mode. **Dietvorst's 2016 follow-up fix**: people will use imperfect algorithms IF allowed to slightly modify the inputs or weights. **Implication for product**: DQI weights must become user-adjustable. Highest-leverage Tier 2 ship; founder-approved 2026-05-10. Pipeline change — needs methodology version bump 2.2.0 → 2.3.0 + regression-test plan + held-out-sample DQI distribution check before/after per CLAUDE.md "modifying the pipeline" rule. Implementation sketch in [docs/paper-grounded-tier-plan-2026-05-10.md](docs/paper-grounded-tier-plan-2026-05-10.md) §T2.1.

4. **First-generation tooling failed because it optimised for data integration, not cognitive debiasing** (Ch 5). Cloverpop required secondary interface (rapid dis-adoption — system-of-record fallacy); Foundry conflated data integration with decision intelligence (avg $2M+ deployment cost); Aera/Peak.ai automated tasks instead of augmenting judgment. **Implication**: ambient capture from email/Slack/VDR is the unlock. Currently we have Drive integration but not deep ambient parsing. Founder-approved 2026-05-10 as Tier 2 ship; substantial — own session.

**Wedge customer empirically grounded** (Ch 7): _"The wedge customer is not the CEO executing a once-in-a-decade platform merger; it is the programmatic operator like Kyle Price."_ Tech tuck-ins are repeat-game high-validity environments where Meehl/Dawes mechanical-model evidence dominates. Platform M&A is low-validity single-N. **Our wedge is the validity class where the algorithmic edge is mathematically largest, not the validity class where headline failure rates are most dramatic.** GTM v3.5 already names mid-market corp dev head as Phase 1 HXC; this paper _upgrades_ that from "founder hypothesis" to "literature-supported structural reasoning." Pitch slide 3 (Why Now) and the wedge brief at [SparringRoomTab](src/components/founder-hub/SparringRoomTab.tsx) `phase1_hxc` tier should both lead with the validity-class argument, not the headline 70-90% number.

## Outreach Intelligence Engine — A/B/C (locked 2026-05-17)

**What it is.** A warm-cold-outreach engine surfaced at the top of the Founder Hub Outreach Hub **Pipeline** section ([IntelBriefPanel](src/components/founder-hub/outreach/IntelBriefPanel.tsx)). It reuses the existing news service + cron dispatcher + the personal-social archetype engine + OutreachArtifact — it is **not** a parallel system, and it is **not** an autonomous outbound bot (human-in-loop; nothing is sent; respects "no cold outbound at scale" + Sharran 1-1-1 + LinkedIn ToS). Three phases, each its own commit, all gates green:

- **Phase A** ([intel-brief.ts](src/lib/outreach/intel-brief.ts), `6869401a`) — nightly corp-dev/M&A digest. `corp_dev` FeedCategory + Crunchbase/PE-Hub feeds (fail-soft; the brief also draws on `business` + SEC `regulatory`). `/api/cron/outreach-intel` runs in the daily dispatcher AFTER `sync-intelligence`; one `OutreachIntelBrief` row per UTC day (`briefDate` unique key = idempotency). Pure select/prompt/parse + 18 vitest. Anti-hallucination: items reference articles by integer index, parser resolves back to a real ingested article (LLM can't invent a source link).
- **Phase B** ([prospect-shortlist.ts](src/lib/outreach/prospect-shortlist.ts), `97d86f30`) — pure persona match (zero extra LLM): sector → case-library Industry → first covering WEDGE_PERSONA → PUBLIC anchor case (failure-class, highest impact) → pre-filled DM_TEMPLATES opener. Persisted into `OutreachIntelBrief.shortlist`. 19 vitest incl. the anti-own-deal structural assertion.
- **Phase C** ([onepager.ts](src/lib/outreach/onepager.ts) + [/api/founder-hub/outreach/onepager](src/app/api/founder-hub/outreach/onepager/route.ts)) — public-case-anchored 1-pager generator. A **sibling** of `/outreach/generate` (NOT a branch of its SSE profile-extraction stream — different input shape, single synchronous gen, lower blast radius) that reuses OutreachArtifact (`intent: 'case_onepager'`, `status: 'draft'`, surfaces in the same pipeline), the personal-social archetype engine (`pickArchetype` / `buildPersonalSocialSystemPrompt`), and Phase B's canonical `selectOnepagerAnchor`. 8 vitest incl. the guardrail.

**The ego-threat lock is STRUCTURAL, not prompt-level.** Every prospect-facing anchor is drawn ONLY from the injected `ALL_CASES` library; there is no prospect-decision input anywhere in the data flow, so the engine is physically incapable of auditing the prospect's own deal. The `buildOnepagerInstruction` HARD RULE additionally forbids the model inventing one ("you were given NO information about {prospectCompany}'s deals — invent none; never audits the reader; 'unaudited reasoning' not broken thinking"). This is the [feedback-cold-outreach-ego-threat-guardrail](memory) made code.

**Forward-looking rules:** (1) new ambient/intel ingestion source → extend `BRIEF_FEED_CATEGORIES` + `CORP_DEV_KEYWORDS`, never re-implement selection. (2) The shortlist/1-pager anchor MUST stay sourced from `ALL_CASES` via the canonical Phase-B helpers — never accept a prospect-supplied case or a free-text "their deal". (3) New persona → the shortlist inherits it via WEDGE_PERSONAS (event-prep SSOT); add a DM_TEMPLATES entry in lockstep. (4) Keep this in the Outreach Hub (the ONE conversion mechanism), never Content Studio (the ONE traffic source) — collapsing them breaks the 1-1-1 discipline. (5) No autonomous send / LinkedIn scrape — if a future ask drifts there, route through the founder; the human-in-loop + no-scale-outbound constraint is load-bearing.

## Wedge conversion ledger (locked 2026-05-18 — the deep-audit #1 finding made code)

**Why it exists.** Every deep-audit (2026-05-18, `audit-2026-05-18.md`) named the same load-bearing pickup: the product is not the bottleneck — the Phase-1 wedge had **zero instrumented prospect entries** with the month-4 kill checkpoint (`<5 paid Individuals by month 4 = halt-and-pivot, regardless of every other metric`, GTM v3.5) ~3.5 months out. GTM v3.5 mandates "track conversion religiously — DMs sent, replies, audit booked, audit completed, conversion." `OutreachArtifact` is an artifact-of-a-moment (the generated DM); this is the **funnel entity**.

**What shipped.** (a) Prisma `WedgeProspect` model + migration `20260518120000_wedge_prospect_conversion_ledger` — founder-scoped (`userId='founder'`), soft link to `OutreachArtifact` (no FK by design — decoupled + schema-drift-tolerant, same discipline as the other soft links). **Founder must `npx prisma migrate deploy`** lock-step with the deploy (the schema-autonomy grant covers adding it; the deploy is the founder's). (b) Pure SSOT [conversion-ledger.ts](src/lib/outreach/conversion-ledger.ts) — `FUNNEL_STAGES` (dm_sent → replied → audit_booked → audit_completed → converted | lost), `isValidStageTransition` (forward-only · `lost` from any active · terminal stays terminal · same-stage no-op), `computeFunnelMetrics` (per-stage counts + conversion rate + stalled-over-`STALL_DAYS` + `killBand` vs `PHASE1_KILL_FLOOR=5`). 15 vitest ([conversion-ledger.test.ts](src/lib/outreach/conversion-ledger.test.ts)). (c) API [/api/founder-hub/outreach/prospects](src/app/api/founder-hub/outreach/prospects/route.ts) (GET+POST) + [/[id]](src/app/api/founder-hub/outreach/prospects/[id]/route.ts) (PATCH+DELETE), founder-pass, audit actions `PROSPECT_CREATED / _STAGE_ADVANCED / _CONVERTED / _LOST / _DELETED`, schema-drift-tolerant (pre-migration → empty list / clear 503, never a 500). (d) [ConversionLedgerPanel](src/components/founder-hub/outreach/ConversionLedgerPanel.tsx) mounted at the **TOP** of the Outreach Hub Pipeline section, ABOVE `IntelBriefPanel`.

**The honest framing is load-bearing — keep it in the chat + the panel copy.** This is the _instrument_, NOT the work. The work is sending the 5-10 personalised DMs/week and logging them here. An empty ledger means the motion is not running — per the founder-context EXECUTION DISCIPLINE, the urge to keep polishing product instead of filling this ledger IS the displacement signal. Do NOT let a future ship add autonomous send / LinkedIn scrape / auto-stage-inference — the human-in-loop + no-scale-outbound + 1-1-1 (Outreach Hub is the ONE conversion mechanism, never Content Studio, never a new tab) constraints are load-bearing.

**Forward-looking rules:** (1) the stage legality + metric math live ONLY in `conversion-ledger.ts` — any surface that moves a prospect MUST call `isValidStageTransition` + `stageTimestampField`, never inline the rule (same drift-class discipline as `validateStageTransition` / `checkOperationalProxyGate`). (2) New funnel stage ⇒ extend `FUNNEL_STAGES` + the `WedgeProspect` timestamp columns + the test suite in lockstep. (3) New persona ⇒ it flows in automatically via `WEDGE_PERSONAS` (event-prep SSOT); the API validates against it + `'other'`. (4) `PHASE1_KILL_FLOOR` mirrors the GTM v3.5 month-4 floor — if the GTM lock changes the floor, edit the const + the prose here in the same commit (doc-sync class).

## Cognitive-entrenchment wedge asset (locked 2026-05-18 — the one net-new signal from the external-market-research eval)

**Why it exists.** A thorough evaluation of an external Grok corp-dev/M&A market-research pass concluded its headline prescription ("evolve DI into a full Deal Lifecycle Orchestrator; narrowness is a weakness") was the incumbent graveyard and the direct inverse of the locked narrow positioning + the 2026-05 defensibility research — explicitly rejected. The eval found exactly **one** genuinely net-new actionable signal worth extracting: the **cognitive-entrenchment / experienced-operator paradox** — the seasoned acquirer who treats every deal as a snowflake ("this one is special, the comparables don't apply") YET reaches for the same rigid playbook every time. This is a validated mid-market corp-dev pain (independently triangulated by the external research + the existing Kyle Price KB quote + the Kahneman & Klein 2009 experience-penalty-in-low-validity finding already locked in CLAUDE.md).

**It is NOT a new bias — and must never become one.** The narrowness of the 22-bias taxonomy IS the moat. Cognitive entrenchment is the **practitioner-vocabulary deployment of DI-B-022 inside-view dominance + overconfidence** as it manifests in experienced operators. The snowflake instinct and the over-applied template are the same reasoning failing in two directions at once. M&A specificity comes from compound-pattern detection + persona-facing framing + the case library, never from new biases (the existing M&A-workflow-native lock).

**What shipped (5-surface founder-facing wedge cascade, NO pipeline / schema / taxonomy change).** (1) [event-prep.ts](src/lib/data/event-prep.ts) — 4th `BiasHook` on `midmarket_corp_dev` (Inside-View Dominance, GE–Alstom 2015 anchor — library-tagged per the M&A case-tagging lock, no fabrication; distinct from the existing WeWork / Daimler-Chrysler / AOL-Time-Warner hooks). (2) [discovery-pitch-toolkit.ts](src/lib/data/discovery-pitch-toolkit.ts) — new signal-keyed `PitchTrigger` + a third `painSignalCue` on the `midmarket_corp_dev` PERSONA_OPENER. (3) [sparring-room-data.ts](src/components/founder-hub/sparring/sparring-room-data.ts) — new `midmarket_corp_dev` × `objection_handler` SCENARIO_TEMPLATE (3-beat ego-safe counter, distinct from the false-precision Dawes/Meehl scenario and the FH-5.2 wrapper scenario). (4) [education-room-data.ts](src/components/founder-hub/education/education-room-data.ts) — `bias_cognitive_entrenchment` flashcard in the `cognitive_biases` deck, placed after DI-B-022, `kahneman_klein` tag. (5) [founder-context.ts](src/app/api/founder-hub/founder-context.ts) — key-objection entry + routing-rule trigger so chat coaching deploys the ego-safe counter.

**The ego-threat discipline is load-bearing — keep it in every surface.** NEVER call an experienced corp-dev team biased or inexperienced — that is the ego-threat that kills the deal (same class as the [feedback-cold-outreach-ego-threat-guardrail](memory) + the "unaudited reasoning not flawed reasoning" pain-framing lock). The counter is always: agree the experience is real → name the PATTERN + cite Kahneman & Klein 2009 → flip to "the audit protects the experience by applying it where it has validity and pressure-tests it where the reference class says it does not." The read→recall→do→defend loop: drill `bias_cognitive_entrenchment` in Education → deploy via the discovery-toolkit PitchTrigger + the event-prep BiasHook → defend in the Sparring objection scenario.

**Deliberately NOT shipped (recorded boundary, not a silent omission — surfaced for founder decision).** A NAMED_PATTERNS entry for cognitive entrenchment was evaluated and deliberately deferred: it is a 10-surface pipeline-adjacent cascade (4 internal pipeline + 6 marketing data + ≥1 case-tagging) and a founder-gated "Modifying the analysis pipeline" change. The pattern is already structurally caught — it is DI-B-022 + overconfidence, which the existing "Reference-Class Blindness" toxic combo already fires on. Promoting it to a first-class named pattern is a separate, founder-routed decision; the wedge-asset cascade above is the correct boil-the-ocean scope for a validated outreach/positioning phrase.

**Forward-looking rule.** When a future external market-research / advisor pass surfaces a validated practitioner pain-phrase, the cascade is these 5 founder-facing surfaces in lockstep (event-prep BiasHook + discovery-toolkit PitchTrigger/cue + Sparring objection scenario + Education flashcard + founder-context routing) — NOT a new bias, NOT a new NAMED_PATTERN, NOT a new persona/archetype (the ranked SSOT sets stay parsimonious). Route any pipeline/taxonomy expansion through the founder; the wedge-surface cascade is the default home for validated language.

## Encryption key resolution fail-closed (locked 2026-05-25 — audit-hardening)

**Why this lock exists.** A 2026-05-25 security audit flagged `getCurrentKeyVersion` in [src/lib/utils/encryption.ts](src/lib/utils/encryption.ts) as a silent-downgrade window. The function had TWO failure modes that returned a version number without verifying a key for it actually existed:

1. **Explicit `_VERSION` set without matching key**: operator bumped `DOCUMENT_ENCRYPTION_KEY_VERSION=2` BEFORE setting `DOCUMENT_ENCRYPTION_KEY_V2`. Function returned 2, downstream `getKeyForVersion(2)` threw with a generic error.
2. **No keys configured at all**: function returned `LEGACY_VERSION` (1), downstream throw at `getKeyForVersion(1)`.

Both paths were technically fail-closed at encrypt time (the downstream throw caught the misconfiguration), but they were silent-downgrade WINDOWS for any future caller that used the version number for purposes beyond an immediate `getKeyForVersion` lookup (e.g. stamping a row's keyVersion column BEFORE the encrypt call).

**The fix.** `getCurrentKeyVersion` now throws fail-closed at the resolution site:

- Explicit `_VERSION=N` without matching `_V{N}` key → throws with "Misconfigured rotation — set the V{N} key BEFORE bumping `_VERSION`" + remediation hint
- No keys at all → throws with "No encryption key configured for domain X. Set `<PREFIX>` or `<PREFIX>_V1`."
- Unparseable `_VERSION` value (e.g. `=abc`) → still warns + falls through to probe (robust against operator typos that don't change substance)

**The standing contradiction.** [encryption.test.ts](src/lib/utils/encryption.test.ts) — 8 new regression tests (21/21 total) lock the fail-closed behavior: happy path / misconfigured rotation / no-keys-at-all / unparseable / probe-fallback / legacy-alias-resolution / end-to-end via `encryptDocumentContent`. If a future refactor returns a version number without verifying its key resolves, the suite breaks.

**Production safety.** All current encrypt-path callers either (a) guard with `isDocumentEncryptionEnabled()` before calling `encryptDocumentContent` (5 routes do this verbatim) or (b) call `encryptToken` inside an OAuth callback where a hard-fail is the correct response when the env var is missing. Slack-callback failure surfaces as "Slack integration error" — the operator sees the diagnostic in logs. No legitimate scenario reaches the throw path.

**Forward-looking rules.**

1. **`getCurrentKeyVersion` is the single point where key-availability is verified during encrypt-time resolution.** When extending the encryption module with new domains or new resolution rules, the invariant is: every return value MUST have a verifiable key. Never return a version number that requires the caller to validate.

2. **Rotation procedure is unchanged.** The 4-step rotation flow at the top of `encryption.ts` still works exactly as documented — set `_V{N}` → bump `_VERSION` → run `npm run rotate:encryption-key` → drop old key. The fail-closed change only fires when steps 1 + 2 are inverted (operator bumps `_VERSION` before setting the new key), which is a misconfiguration the function now diagnoses clearly instead of letting downstream code surface generically.

3. **The unparseable-VERSION fall-through is INTENTIONAL robustness, not a gap.** When `_VERSION=2foo` is set, `parseInt` returns 2 — the misconfigured-rotation check fires correctly. When `_VERSION=abc` is set, it logs a warn and falls through to the probe (which finds the right key regardless). This is the "typo recovery" path; do not "fix" it by throwing — that would brittle the rotation workflow without security benefit.

## BiasTask PATCH authorization-matrix lock (locked 2026-05-25 — false-positive audit response)

**Why this lock exists.** A 2026-05-24 security audit flagged the BiasTask PATCH outer gate at [src/app/api/bias-tasks/[id]/route.ts](src/app/api/bias-tasks/[id]/route.ts) as a privilege escalation — claiming `if (!isCreator && !isAssignee && !isOrgAdmin && !isOrgMember)` is "effectively `if (false)` for any org member" and that "other PATCH fields (title / description / dueAt) gate ONLY on the outer check." **The audit was wrong.** Every per-field write in the handler carries an explicit inner gate (`isCreator || isOrgAdmin` for title/description/dueAt/reassign; `isAssignee || isCreator || isOrgAdmin` for status/resolutionNote) that runs BEFORE the prisma.update call. The outer gate is **tenant-isolation**, not write-permission — it rejects strangers with no relationship to the task's org.

**The standing contradiction.** [bias-task-patch.test.ts](src/app/api/bias-tasks/[id]/bias-task-patch.test.ts) — 24 tests that lock the per-field authorization matrix. The false-positive proof block ("PATCH /api/bias-tasks/:id — org member without creator/assignee/admin role") demonstrates that an org member who is NOT creator/assignee/admin returns 403 on title / description / dueAt / reassign / status edit attempts. If a future audit re-raises the same flag without updating these tests first, the tests are the standing rebuttal.

**The authorization matrix (the design contract).**

| Field                       | Required role                    |
| --------------------------- | -------------------------------- |
| `status`                    | assignee \| creator \| org admin |
| `assigneeUserId` (reassign) | creator \| org admin             |
| `title`                     | creator \| org admin             |
| `description`               | creator \| org admin             |
| `dueAt`                     | creator \| org admin             |
| `resolutionNote`            | assignee \| creator \| org admin |

**Forward-looking rules.**

1. **When extending the PATCH handler with a new field, add the inner gate FIRST.** The inline comment on the outer gate names this discipline. Every new body field needs its own `if (!<allowed-role>) return 403` BEFORE the `updates.<field> = ...` line. The outer gate does NOT enforce write-permission and must never be relied on for that.

2. **When refactoring the outer gate, do not drop the test suite.** The 24 tests are intentionally redundant with the code's structure — they exist to defend against an inverse refactor (e.g. someone "simplifying" the outer gate in a way that removes the per-field inner gates). If the outer gate is restructured (the redundant `!isOrgAdmin && !isOrgMember` is logically simplifiable since `isOrgMember = isOrgAdmin || ...`), keep every per-field test passing.

3. **This lock is the canonical response pattern for false-positive audits.** When an audit raises a security flag that turns out to be wrong on close reading, the response is: (a) prove the diagnostic in an authorization-matrix test class that locks the actual behavior, (b) add an inline comment to the handler explaining why the apparent vulnerability is intentional / not a vulnerability, (c) document the false-positive class in CLAUDE.md so future audits inherit the conclusion. Do NOT close as "wontfix" — that drops the protective shield. The test suite IS the shield.

## Fund-launch container mode — Adaptation #3 (locked 2026-05-24, same-day follow-up to Adaptation #2)

**What it is.** The 3rd Sankore product adaptation in 24 hours (after Retroactive audit mode #1 + real_estate_development #2). Adds the **5th** `DecisionContainer` kind: **`fund_launch`** — launching a new fund vehicle with a 6-stage lifecycle (thesis_development → target_market_sizing → fee_structure → anchor_lp_commitments → regulatory_filing → go_to_market). Founder-approved 2026-05-24 as the natural completion of the CONTAINER_MODES expansion before Adaptation #5 (multi-decision-class portfolio dashboard) ships, since the dashboard surfaces all kinds and more modes shipped = more value. Sankore launches funds repeatedly (Agriculture Fund, Real Wealth Fund); the immediate utility is real.

**Architecture (same boolean-extension pattern as Adaptation #2).** Pure additive change to `src/lib/data/decision-container-modes.ts`: `DecisionContainerKind` union extends to 5, `CONTAINER_MODES` map gains a 5th entry, `CONTAINER_KINDS` array gains 'fund_launch', `ContainerOutcomeShape.shape` union extends to 5 with `'fund_realisation'`. 68 vitest assertions enforce the 5-mode contract (was 58 at the 4-mode lock; +10 for fund_launch). No Prisma migration — `DecisionContainer.kind` is a String column that accepts arbitrary values. No pipeline change. Same R²F audit pipeline, same DPR, same composite DQI, same Brier-scored outcome calibration across all five modes.

**6-stage lifecycle (committee gate at anchor LP commitments).** `thesis_development` (pre_committee) → `target_market_sizing` (pre_committee) → `fee_structure` (pre_committee) → `anchor_lp_commitments` (**committee_gate** — the audit moment R²F fires hardest on; required docs: thesis_memo + fund_prospectus + lp_ask_deck) → `regulatory_filing` (post_committee) → `go_to_market` (post_committee). Why anchor LP commitments is the committee gate: the first-close anchor commitment is the moment LPs (typically DFIs or strategic anchors) put real money against the thesis under real procurement-grade scrutiny. Regulatory filing comes AFTER because most jurisdictions allow parallel-track filing, but committing capital first crystallises the decision. Per-stage `likelyPatternLabels` reference canonical NAMED_PATTERNS (no new toxic combination shipped — the existing taxonomy covers fund-launch failure modes: Optimism Trap on AUM ramp, Anchoring Trap on prior-fund returns, Echo Chamber on thesis confirmation, Halo Effect on anchor-LP halo, Recency Spiral on TAM extrapolation).

**New `fund_realisation` outcome shape.** Primary metric: realised AUM as % of target at final close. Full shape: `realised_aum_pct` (percent, primary) + `final_close_months` (months from first close to final close) + `anchor_lp_count` + `total_lp_count` + `realised_fund_irr` (long-horizon, often too-early) + `realised_dpi` (distributions to paid-in) + `realised_tvpi` (total value to paid-in) + `verdict` + `notes`. Captures both the fundraise outcome (AUM hit, time to close, LP count) AND the long-horizon fund performance (IRR/DPI/TVPI). Most fund-launch containers will have only the fundraise outcome populated initially; IRR/DPI/TVPI fill in over the 5-10 year fund life via the per-container outcome capture flow.

**4 new doc subtypes added to `INVESTMENT_DOCUMENT_TYPES`** with DOC_TYPE_OVERLAYS for each: `thesis_memo` (prior-fund anchoring / TAM extrapolation / "why us, why now" ungrounded / sourcing-edge claims / comparable-fund blindspot), `fund_prospectus` (GP track-record curation / fee-structure opacity / conflicts-of-interest disclosure / key-person risk / target-return hedging), `lp_ask_deck` (narrative-coherence overfitting / commitment-momentum anchoring / "strategic LP" halo / track-record visual curation / "why this vintage" ungrounded), `regulatory_filing` (disclosure-consistency gaps / key-person disclosure completeness / conflicts-of-interest filing / jurisdiction-specific gates / timing-of-filing-vs-fundraise). Each overlay names canonical failure patterns the bias detective should map onto.

**Sample bundle** for the `pe_vc` role: `PE_PAN_AFRICAN_AGRICULTURE_FUND_LAUNCH` ([sample-bundles.ts](src/lib/data/sample-bundles.ts) — synthetic anonymised Pan-African agriculture-vintage fund-launch thesis memo, ~700 words. Targets $120M AUM for Vintage I across Nigeria/Ghana/Kenya/Tanzania. Embeds Anchoring (target IRR matches prior-fund 24% without scaling adjustment for new fund size + vintage) / Optimism (TAM extrapolation 6.8% CAGR with straight-line growth) / Recency (AfCFTA single-market provisions as primary tailwind without acknowledging the cycle) / Confirmation (every claim supports the thesis without counter-evidence) / Halo (DFI anchor commits used as halo for follow-on LPs) biases. Expected DQI 46. Procurement-grade memo that survives a sophisticated-LP smell test.

**Persona defaults UNCHANGED.** `defaultContainerKindForRole` in [useContainers.ts](src/hooks/useContainers.ts) keeps the prior mapping. `fund_launch` users pick explicitly because fund-launch is an OCCASIONAL event for a GP whose daily workflow is investment OUT of an existing fund. Smaller-fund GPs don't relaunch a new fund every week — the persona-default correctly anchors them on `investment`; when they decide to launch a new fund, they pick `fund_launch` explicitly.

**Gates green at ship.** tsc clean. 1278/1278 vitest pass (was 1268 at the Adaptation #2 lock — +10 from the fund_launch describe block + helper assertions extended). silent-catches 198 at baseline. count-drift 73 at baseline. canonical-imports clean. positioning clean. Prettier clean. slop-scan scorePerKloc under 4.0 trip-wire.

**Forward-looking rules.**

1. **5-mode cascade is now the canonical SSOT extension pattern.** Going from 3 → 4 → 5 modes in 24 hours validated the boolean-extension architecture. The next mode (if ever — there's no Adaptation #6 in the SankoreBrief queue today) would follow the same shape: extend `DecisionContainerKind` union, add `<KIND>_MODE` const, add to `CONTAINER_MODES`, extend `CONTAINER_KINDS`, extend `ContainerOutcomeShape.shape` union if needed, add new doc subtypes to `INVESTMENT_DOCUMENT_TYPES` with matching DOC_TYPE_OVERLAYS, add a sample bundle, update the SSOT header, extend the vitest suite ("exactly N modes — kind list..." + describe block).
