2. **Drift class to watch on every mode extension.** Three sites needed manual updating across the 3→4→5 transitions: `useContainers.ts` JSDoc (mode count), `AiNativeMatrix.tsx` `diSource` (mode count), and founder-context.ts chat preamble (mode names + vitest assertion count + section header). The 4-mode lock caught these via my own grep; the 5-mode lock caught them again in the same places. Future audits should grep `rg "(three|four|five|3|4|5)\s+(modes|kinds|container)"` across `src/` after any CONTAINER_MODES extension to verify no stale prose references slip past.

3. **DOC_TYPE_OVERLAYS for new doc subtypes MUST name canonical failure patterns.** The 4 new fund-launch overlays each reference at least 2-4 NAMED_PATTERNS (Optimism Trap, Anchoring Trap, Echo Chamber, Halo Effect, Yes Committee, Sunk Ship, Deadline Panic) so the bias detective routes consistently with the rest of the pipeline. When extending overlays for any future vertical, follow the same shape: failure-mode bullets + "NAMED TOXIC COMBINATIONS to flag" footer naming the canonical patterns.

4. **No autonomous fundraise-outcome inference, ever.** When a container's outcome is logged with only the fundraise metrics (realised_aum_pct, final_close_months, anchor_lp_count, total_lp_count) populated and the long-horizon metrics (realised_fund_irr, realised_dpi, realised_tvpi) absent, the verdict is correctly "too_early_to_tell" — never auto-infer fund-level performance from fundraise success. A successful fundraise tells you the GP could attract capital, NOT that the fund will return capital. Surface "fundraise outcome captured · fund-level outcome pending" framing in any UI consumer that surfaces the verdict.

## Real-estate development container mode — Adaptation #2 (locked 2026-05-24)

**What it is.** The 2nd Sankore product adaptation. Adds a 4th `DecisionContainer` kind alongside investment / acquisition / strategic: **`real_estate_development`** — ground-up or major-reposition real-estate projects with a 6-stage lifecycle (site_acquisition → entitlement → financing → construction → leasing → stabilization). Founder-approved 2026-05-24 as boil-the-ocean follow-up to Adaptation #1 (Retroactive audit mode). Sankore's portfolio includes multiple active real-estate projects; the existing 3 modes did not fit a mixed-use development proposal — financing-close is structurally different from an IC vote on a portfolio investment or an M&A board review.

**Architecture (boolean-extension, not refactor).** Pure additive change to `src/lib/data/decision-container-modes.ts`: `DecisionContainerKind` union extends, `CONTAINER_MODES` map gains a 4th entry, `CONTAINER_KINDS` array gains 'real_estate_development', `ContainerOutcomeShape.shape` union extends to `'irr_moic' | 'synergy_realisation' | 'forecast_hit_rate' | 'dev_yield'`. Type-system + 58 vitest assertions enforce the 4-mode contract loudly (was 36 at the 3-mode lock). No Prisma migration — `DecisionContainer.kind` is a String column that already accepts arbitrary values. No pipeline change — same R²F audit pipeline, same DPR, same composite DQI, same Brier-scored outcome calibration across all four modes.

**6-stage lifecycle (committee gate at financing close).** `site_acquisition` (pre_committee) → `entitlement` (pre_committee) → `financing` (**committee_gate** — the audit moment R²F fires hardest on; required docs: site_analysis + financial_pro_forma + regulatory_checklist) → `construction` (post_committee) → `leasing` (post_committee) → `stabilization` (post_committee). Per-stage `likelyPatternLabels` reference canonical NAMED_PATTERNS (no new toxic-combination shipped — the existing taxonomy covers RE failure modes: Optimism Trap on lease-up timing, Anchoring on cap rates, Sunk Ship on entitlement spend, Doubling Down on hold-rather-than-exit, Recency Spiral on hot-cycle comparable sets).

**New `dev_yield` outcome shape.** Primary metric: realised project IRR. Full shape: `realised_irr` (percent, primary) + `equity_multiple` + `cost_overrun_pct` + `schedule_overrun_months` + `stabilized_noi` + `months_to_stabilization` + `verdict` (value_created / value_neutral / value_destroyed / too_early_to_tell) + `notes`. The shape is consumed only inside the SSOT + test today — no downstream Brier-scoring branches on shape, so adding the 4th outcome shape is structurally safe. When per-shape Brier specialisation lands, every consumer reads from `outcomeShape.shape`.

**5 new doc subtypes added to `INVESTMENT_DOCUMENT_TYPES`** (the canonical doc-type registry — naming is historical, the array is mode-agnostic): `site_analysis`, `financial_pro_forma`, `regulatory_checklist`, `contractor_selection`, `appraisal`. Each gains a `DOC_TYPE_OVERLAYS` prompt that instructs the bias detective on real-estate-specific failure patterns: (a) site_analysis — anchoring to hot-cycle comparables, demand-absorption optimism, demographic extrapolation, comp cherry-picking, missing downside data; (b) financial_pro_forma — terminal cap-rate anchoring, lease-up timing optimism, construction-cost under-reservation, interest-rate assumption gaming, sensitivity-table completeness, hidden promote/waterfall mechanics; (c) regulatory_checklist — zoning/entitlement risk minimisation, environmental review shortcuts, community-opposition underweighting, timeline optimism, missing jurisdiction-specific gates (especially Pan-African layers); (d) contractor_selection — bid-comparison cherry-picking, lowest-bidder anchoring, schedule optimism, change-order governance, contingency-use rules, contract-structure / project-risk mismatch; (e) appraisal — commissioning-party bias, comparable-selection bias, cap-rate anchoring, income-approach optimism, highest-and-best-use assumptions.

**Sample bundle** for the `pe_vc` role: `PE_LAGOS_MIXED_USE_DEVELOPMENT` ([sample-bundles.ts](src/lib/data/sample-bundles.ts) — synthetic anonymised 14-storey Victoria Island mixed-use development memo, ~700 words, with embedded Anchoring (exit cap at today's compressed 7.5% projected 5 years forward) / Optimism (18-month lease-up in a sub-market that historically averages 24-30) / Sunk Cost ("$1.2M entitlement cannot be re-tendered") / Recency (comp set drawn entirely from 2023-2024) / Confirmation biases. Expected DQI 47. Procurement-grade memo that survives a skeptical-reader smell test.

**Persona defaults UNCHANGED.** `defaultContainerKindForRole` in [useContainers.ts](src/hooks/useContainers.ts) maps by LEGACY role: pe_vc / cso → 'investment', ma → 'acquisition', bizops → 'strategic'. Through the v3.5 persona→role bridge (`phase1PersonaToOnboardingRole` in icp.ts): small-fund GP / fractional CSO → 'investment', mid-market corp dev head → 'acquisition', **PE-backed founder → 'acquisition'** (maps to `ma` — "their primary memo workflow is acquisitions + IC" per the icp.ts mapping rationale; a prior version of this prose wrongly said 'strategic', corrected 2026-06-11), bizops → 'strategic'. `real_estate_development` users pick explicitly because Sankore-style mixed-business-line operators move across modes; no single legacy role correctly defaults to real-estate. The kind picker on `/dashboard/decisions/new` automatically surfaces "Real-Estate Development" as a 4th option (`CONTAINER_KINDS` array auto-extends, the picker reads from `CONTAINER_MODES`).

**Gates green at ship.** tsc clean. 1268/1268 vitest pass (was 1259 — +9 from the real-estate-development describe block + helper assertions extended). silent-catches 198 at baseline. count-drift 73 at baseline. canonical-imports clean. positioning clean. Prettier clean. slop-scan scorePerKloc under 4.0 trip-wire. AEO audit em-dash sweep also shipped in the same commit (FAQ 9→1, Glossary 5→1, Compare 3→1 user-visible em-dashes).

**Forward-looking rules.**

1. **The cascade discipline scales to N modes.** When Adaptation #3 (fund_launch) ships, the same pattern applies: extend `DecisionContainerKind` union, add a `FUND_LAUNCH_MODE` definition, add to `CONTAINER_MODES`, extend `CONTAINER_KINDS`, extend `ContainerOutcomeShape.shape` union if needed, add new doc subtypes to `INVESTMENT_DOCUMENT_TYPES` with matching `DOC_TYPE_OVERLAYS`, add a sample bundle, update the SSOT header to "five modes", update the cross-mode invariant assertions in the test suite ("exactly N modes — kind list..."). The 4-mode lock made the 5-mode cascade structurally clearer; the 3→4 transition itself caught two drift sites (`useContainers.ts` JSDoc + `AiNativeMatrix.tsx` `diSource`) — both now reference the kind count without literal numbers where possible.

2. **No new NAMED_PATTERNS in this ship — by design.** Adding a real-estate-specific named pattern is the 10-surface marketing+pipeline cascade per CLAUDE.md "Modifying the analysis pipeline" rule; founder-gated. The existing 13 patterns (10 cross-domain + 3 M&A) cover real-estate failure modes adequately via Optimism Trap / Anchoring + (existing patterns ending in Doubling Down + Sunk Ship). A future real-estate-specific pattern (e.g. "The Stabilization Stretch" — Optimism + Anchoring + Sunk Cost on lease-up timing in a development project where entitlement spend is sunk) would ship via the same cascade as Synergy Mirage / Conglomerate Fallacy / Winner's Curse.

3. **The `dev_yield` outcome shape is internal-only today.** Brier-scoring doesn't branch on shape — the `realised_irr` primary metric is scored the same way as `moic` (both numeric, both `primary: true`). If per-shape Brier specialisation lands (e.g. real-estate `realised_irr` should be Brier-scored against the IRR target with a specific calibration curve), every consumer reads from `outcomeShape.shape`; never hardcode the shape comparison.

4. **DOC_TYPE_OVERLAYS for new doc subtypes MUST name canonical failure patterns.** The 5 new RE overlays each reference at least 2-3 NAMED_PATTERNS (Optimism Trap, Anchoring Trap, Sunk Ship, Yes Committee) so the bias detective routes consistently with the rest of the pipeline. When extending overlays for any new vertical (Adaptation #3 fund_launch, future), follow the same shape: failure-mode bullets + "NAMED TOXIC COMBINATIONS to flag" footer naming the canonical patterns the overlay's bias-detection should map onto.

## Retroactive audit mode — Adaptation #1 (locked 2026-05-21, the Sankore-killer feature)

**What it is.** The first of the 5 Sankore product adaptations. Runs DI's audit pipeline against historical CLOSED decisions where outcomes are already known — populates Bias Genome / Decision DNA / Knowledge Graph with REAL longitudinal data immediately, not over 12 months of forward use. Compresses 12 months of forward calibration into days of retroactive backfill. Live entry: [/dashboard/decisions/retroactive](<src/app/(platform)/dashboard/decisions/retroactive/page.tsx>). Founder-approved 2026-05-21 with explicit boil-the-ocean instruction + full architecture latitude.

**Architecture (boolean flag, NOT new container kind).** A boolean `isRetroactive` on the existing `DecisionContainer` model composes with all 3 kinds (investment / acquisition / strategic). Sankore's 30-50 historical decisions span all three; a new kind would force a triple cascade for zero gain. The boolean is additive Prisma migration `20260521120000_retroactive_audit_mode` (with sparse index `WHERE "isRetroactive" = true` for analytics) — pre-2026-05-21 rows default `false` + behave as forward containers, fully schema-drift-tolerant. Two new fields land: `isRetroactive Boolean @default(false)` + `retroactiveMetadata Json?` (decidedAt + outcomeKnownAt + sourceProvenance + bulkUploadBatchId + pairingConfidence + pairingMethod).

**Two-tier outcome extraction.** Pure deterministic Tier 1 (regex over 12+ canonical outcome patterns covering exit/sale, IRR/MOIC, synergies, write-downs, deal-failed, project-abandoned, bankruptcy, mixed, too-early signals + METRIC_PATTERNS for IRR / MOIC / synergy-% / exit amount / write-down amount / fund return / time-to-exit) always runs first — free, fast, never fabricates. Tier 2 LLM via deepseek-v4-flash through the Vercel AI Gateway (`MODEL_RECOMMENDATIONS`) augments by refining narrative + adding evidence quotes + boosting confidence, but `validateLlmQuotes` enforces every evidence quote is a verbatim substring of the source content (prevents hallucination). When Tier 1 confidence ≥ 0.6, the verdict is locked — LLM can refine but cannot override. AI_GATEWAY_API_KEY absent → Tier 1 returned unchanged. Endpoint: [/api/retroactive/extract-outcome](src/app/api/retroactive/extract-outcome/route.ts) (Supabase SSR auth, 30/min user + 500/hr global rate-limits).

**Bulk pairing engine.** Pure-function ([bulkPairing.ts](src/lib/retroactive/bulkPairing.ts)) over uploaded historical docs. Confidence = `(entityOverlap × 0.5) + (temporalProximityScore × 0.25) + (contentSimilarity × 0.25)`. Codename overlap weighted 2× over org-name overlap (project codenames are stronger signals). Temporal sweet spot 6mo-3yr → score 1.0; outcome-BEFORE-memo → 0; > 10yr → 0. Greedy stable matching: sort all memo×outcome candidates by confidence descending, assign each outcome to at most one memo. Mixed-role docs (a single "Decision Review" containing both decision + outcome) self-pair at 0.9. Confidence bands per `PAIRING_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLDS`: `auto_high` ≥ 0.75 (one-click confirm), `auto_medium` ≥ 0.50 (review signals), `auto_low` ≥ 0.25 (manual triage), `unpaired` < 0.25 (memo with no outcome → fill by hand). Multipart upload endpoint at [/api/retroactive/bulk-upload](src/app/api/retroactive/bulk-upload/route.ts) — caps mirror Sankore expectations: 30 files / 50MB total / 100B min per file / 5 bulks/hr/user / 60s timeout. Per file: `parseFile()` → `detectDocumentRole` → `extractEntities` → `inferDocumentDate` → Document.create (encrypted if `isDocumentEncryptionEnabled()`).

**Container API extension.** [/api/containers](src/app/api/containers/route.ts) POST accepts three new optional fields: `isRetroactive: boolean`, `retroactiveMetadata` (typed shape), `outcomeOnCreate` (summary + metrics + realisedDqi). When `isRetroactive === true`, integrity gate enforces: retroactiveMetadata present + decidedAt + outcomeKnownAt + outcomeOnCreate.summary (≥ 10 chars). Container creates with `isRetroactive: true` + `retroactiveMetadata` JSON + `decidedAt` stamped from the HISTORICAL date (not "now"). Retroactive containers default to the FINAL committee-gate stage (they're past every pre-committee gate). The `DecisionContainerOutcome` row is created in the same flow with the supplied summary + metrics validated against the SSOT `mode.outcomeShape.fields` (typed coercion: percent / number / currency / months parsed to float; enum / text passed verbatim). `recomputeContainerMetrics(id)` fires immediately so container-level aggregations sharpen on day one. New audit-log action `CONTAINER_RETROACTIVE_CREATED` (+ `CONTAINER_RETROACTIVE_BULK_UPLOAD` reserved for the bulk-upload route).

**The "no 90-day wait" property.** The outcome row is created at container-create time, so when the memo document is then attached and the audit pipeline runs on it, the recalibration trigger on `/api/analyze/stream` reads the EXISTING outcome row and grounds against KNOWN reality rather than forecasted priors. This is the Vector 1 extension: the operational-proxy calibration loop (shipped 2026-05-17 — forced ≤90-day proxies at vote time) closes here on day one for historical decisions, because the proxy WAS the outcome and it's already settled.

**UI (3-step wizard).** Composed of three components in [src/components/retroactive/](src/components/retroactive/) + a page at [/dashboard/decisions/retroactive](<src/app/(platform)/dashboard/decisions/retroactive/page.tsx>). Step 1: `BulkUploadDropzone` drag-and-drop with per-file removal, byte/file caps mirrored from server, "Run pairing engine" submits multipart FormData. Step 2: `RetroactivePairingReview` renders the result grouped by confidence band, expandable per-pair signals row (entity overlap % / time gap days / content similarity %) + draft outcome narrative when present, dismiss / "Create container →" per pair. Step 3: `RetroactiveContainerForm` modal for a single pair — kind picker + name (pre-filled from filename) + decisionFrame + targetCompany + sector + decidedAt + outcomeKnownAt + sourceProvenance + outcome summary + per-field metric inputs (dynamic from `mode.outcomeShape.fields`, pre-filled from `outcomeDraft.draftMetrics` when match). Wizard tracks confirmed pair ids in a Set; created containers accumulate in a list with deep-link back to the kanban.

**Discoverability.** Three entry points: (a) [/dashboard/decisions](<src/app/(platform)/dashboard/decisions/page.tsx>) header gains a secondary "Backfill historical" button (Clock3 icon) sibling to the primary "New decision" CTA — visible to any user working out of the kanban; (b) [CommandPalette](src/components/ui/CommandPalette.tsx) `decisions-retroactive` entry with keywords `retroactive` / `historical` / `backfill` / `bulk upload` / `sankore retroactive` / `bias genome populate` / `no 90 day wait` — surfaces via ⌘K; (c) [SankoreBrief FiveAdaptations](src/components/founder-hub/sankore/FiveAdaptations.tsx) shows "Open live surface →" CTA when `ProductAdaptation.liveRoute` is set (new optional field on the type) — the brief becomes self-actionable.

**Lint + test posture at ship.** tsc clean. 1259/1259 vitest pass (49 new retroactive tests across outcomeExtractor + entityExtractor + bulkPairing — none added to the codebase total because vitest re-discovers them; the 1259 figure is the combined post-ship count). silent-catch baseline 195 → 198 (+3 ALL canonical req.json()/res.json() body-parse class — 1 in extract-outcome route + 1 in BulkUploadDropzone + 1 in RetroactiveContainerForm; each annotated inline; no delivery/audit/flywheel write swallowed — the container-create call fails-closed with a 500 + dev-mode diagnostic). count-drift 73 / canonical-imports / positioning all clean. Prettier clean. slop-scan scorePerKloc under 4.0.

**Forward-looking rules.**

1. **Boolean flag composition is canonical for cross-mode product variants.** When a future product variant spans all 3 (or N) container kinds and ADDS metadata rather than swapping the workflow, default to a boolean flag + a JSON metadata column — never a new kind. New kinds belong to fundamentally different workflows (the existing investment/acquisition/strategic split; the queued real_estate_development + fund_launch in Adaptations #2-3).

2. **Tier 1 always runs first; Tier 2 is augmentation, never replacement.** When extending the outcome extractor for new domains (real-estate developments, fund launches), add a new pure-function regex tier first, then optionally a Tier 2 LLM augmentation that validates substrings against source. Never trust LLM-claimed evidence quotes — every quote must verbatim-match the input or fall back to Tier 1.

3. **Bulk pairing weights are tunable per-domain.** The 0.5 entity / 0.25 temporal / 0.25 content weights are calibrated for VC/PE/corp-dev decisions where org names + project codenames are strong signals. For domains where entities matter less (e.g. pure-strategy memos with no named counterparty), surface a per-domain weight override on `PairingInput` rather than forking the engine. Same canonical-import discipline as DQI weights.

4. **The Bias Genome / Decision DNA / Knowledge Graph trigger path is per-analysis, NOT per-container.** Creating the container + outcome row at retroactive-create time does NOT yet propagate to the cross-org Bias Genome — that happens when the memo doc is attached to the container, the audit pipeline runs, the analysis lands, and the `/api/analyze/stream` recalibration trigger reads the outcome row + fires `recalibrateFromOutcome` which then stamps Brier + writes `Analysis.recalibratedDqi`. The retroactive shipping closes the loop on day one because the outcome IS there at audit time. If a future change moves recalibration off the per-analysis path, the retroactive flow needs explicit re-wiring.

5. **No autonomous outcome fabrication, ever.** If Tier 1 returns no signals AND no outcome document was paired, the user fills in the outcome manually via the form — the system never invents one. The retroactive flow only earns the moat if every container reflects a REAL decision with a REAL outcome the founder can defend in a procurement meeting. Surface a future "auto-extract from memo body" temptation as a founder-routed decision, never a silent ship.

6. **Per CLAUDE.md "Modifying the analysis pipeline" rule, the per-analysis recalibration trigger stays unchanged in this ship.** Adaptation #1 only adds the entry point for backfilling and the container-level outcome row. The downstream pipeline path is unchanged. When future adaptations need to change the per-analysis trigger (e.g. to surface confidence bands on a recalibration UI), route through the founder.

## Faith OS "Today's Three" — daily-priority goal setting (locked 2026-06-01)

**What it is.** The operating-system layer of Faith OS — the founder's daily productivity ritual woven into the Foundations tab (not a separate surface). Research-grounded: the right number of daily priorities is small, and for most people it is THREE. The cap of three IS the feature, enforced server-side. Founder-approved "boil the ocean" build (research → SSOT → schema → API → UI → tests → docs in one ship). Mounted in [FaithOSTab](src/components/founder-hub/FaithOSTab.tsx) directly after the Daily Spiritual Checkin, so the day's planning sits inside the devotional loop, not beside it.

**The research it operationalises** (named, verifiable; the un-sourced 5/25 rule is flagged "attributed" the way the codebase flags every un-proven number): working-memory limits ~4±1 (Cowan 2001) + decision fatigue → small lists; the Rule of 3 (Meier 2010; Bailey 2016); specific+challenging beats "do your best" in ~90% of studies (Locke & Latham goal-setting theory); if-then implementation intentions roughly double follow-through (Gollwitzer 1999; WOOP/MCII, Oettingen); focus on the vital few + the ONE Thing (Buffett 5/25 attributed; Keller & Papasan 2013; Knapp & Zeratsky's daily Highlight 2018). Each is paired with the scriptural frame that makes it hold under pressure (Prov 16:3 commit; Matt 6:33 priority-order; Ps 90:12 number our days; Luke 10:42 "one thing necessary"; Daniel 1:8 resolve-before-pressure) — the same SUCCESS_SCRIPTURE_MAP discipline.

**The four load-bearing design choices:**

1. **Three is a hard cap, server-enforced.** [/api/founder-os/daily-goals](src/app/api/founder-os/daily-goals/route.ts) POST counts ACTIVE (open|done) goals for the date and rejects the 4th with a 400 that says so. `carried` + `released` free their slot. The cap is the point — it forces the choice the long list lets you avoid.
2. **`released` is the agency-surrender beat made concrete.** Status `open | done | carried | released`. Releasing a goal is held-with-open-hands (Prov 16:9 / James 4:13-15), recorded honestly — NOT a missed box. The streak rewards SHOWING UP (setting the three), not perfection, per the anti-prosperity guardrail — completion + highlight-hit are surfaced as separate rates so the two signals never collapse into one guilt metric.
3. **The if-then intention (Gollwitzer) is a first-class field**, and one goal can be starred the Highlight (Keller/Knapp) — one Highlight per day, enforced server-side (POST/PATCH demote the day's other highlight).
4. **"Commit today's three to the Lord" (Prov 16:3)** is a recorded daily act (`committed` per goal), the planning sibling of the prayer journal's answered-prayer record — identity grounding, never a success metric.

**Files.** Prisma model `FounderOsDailyGoal` (additive migration [20260601120000_founder_os_daily_goals](prisma/migrations/20260601120000_founder_os_daily_goals/migration.sql) — new table only, zero-risk; **founder must `npx prisma migrate deploy`** lock-step with deploy, same pattern as every FounderOs\* model) · route [daily-goals/route.ts](src/app/api/founder-os/daily-goals/route.ts) (GET/POST/PATCH/DELETE, `authenticateFounderOs` dual-gate, no audit logging — consistent with every other founder-os route) · teaching SSOT in [faith-os/content.ts](src/components/founder-hub/faith-os/content.ts) (`DAILY_THREE_MAX` + `DAILY_THREE_PRINCIPLES` + `DAILY_THREE_COMMIT` + `DAILY_THREE_RITUAL` + `WHY_THREE`) · pure math [faith-os/daily-three.ts](src/components/founder-hub/faith-os/daily-three.ts) (`summarizeDailyThree` — streak/completion/highlight-hit/heatmap, 13 vitest in [daily-three.test.ts](src/components/founder-hub/faith-os/daily-three.test.ts)) · UI `DailyThreeSection` + GoalRow + AddGoalForm + WhyThreePanel + DailyThreeStatStrip + DailyThreeHeatmap in [FaithOSTab.tsx](src/components/founder-hub/FaithOSTab.tsx).

**Gates green at ship.** tsc clean · 20/20 faith-os vitest (13 new daily-three + 7 existing progress) · positioning clean · counts at baseline 73 · canonical-imports clean · silent-catches 212 (+2, canonical body-parse class) · prettier clean · slop-scan 3.23 (< 4.0).

**Forward-looking rules.**

1. **`DAILY_THREE_MAX` is the single source of the cap** — the route + the helper both import it; never inline `3`. If the cap ever changes (it should not — three is the research-backed number), edit the SSOT only and the API + math + tests follow.
2. **The cap counts only `open` + `done` (active commitments).** Any new status that should be a live commitment must be added to BOTH `ACTIVE_STATUSES` in the route AND `isActive()` in `daily-three.ts` in lockstep — they MUST agree on what "the three" means.
3. **No autonomous goal generation, ever.** The founder writes the three. An AI "suggest today's three from your calendar/inbox" temptation is a founder-routed decision, never a silent ship — the daily commit is HIS act, the same discipline as the no-autonomous-outcome-fabrication rule.
4. **The streak rewards showing up, not perfection** — never reframe it as a completion streak; completion + highlight-hit are deliberately separate rates (anti-prosperity guardrail). When the teaching content evolves, edit the content SSOT; the UI reads it.

### Deepen + tracking layer (locked 2026-06-01 — founder-approved boil-the-ocean follow-up)

Founder picked "deepen Today's Three" + "tracking + weekly review" and directed: **modify existing surfaces, do NOT add another tab** (the Start Here tab already exists; never spawn a parallel one). Everything below extends Faith OS (the operating heart) + the existing Founder OS Sunday weekly review — zero new tabs, zero customer-surface touch, zero pipeline touch.

**Deepen — the cascade + reflection + carry + time-block.**

1. **The cascade (Rule of 3 as a hierarchy).** New `FounderOsPeriodGoal` model (`period: 'week'|'quarter'`, `periodKey`) — a few quarter rocks → ≤3 weekly intentions → the day's three. Cap of three enforced server-side per (userId, period, periodKey) via [/api/founder-os/period-goals](src/app/api/founder-os/period-goals/route.ts). Keys + labels are pure helpers in [faith-os/period-goals.ts](src/components/founder-hub/faith-os/period-goals.ts) (`weekKeyFor` = Sunday-start ISO to match the app's Sunday-week convention; `quarterKeyFor` = `YYYY-Qn`). `PERIOD_GOAL_MAX = DAILY_THREE_MAX` (locked together — the whole cascade obeys one Rule of 3). Rendered as `CascadeSection` (This quarter + This week) ABOVE Today's Three in FaithOSTab.
2. **Cascade link (the clarity unlock).** Additive nullable `FounderOsDailyGoal.linkedPeriodGoalId` (soft ref, no FK — dangling id = "no link"). A daily goal can be set to "serve" a weekly intention via a picker in `GoalRow`; the day's work visibly ladders up instead of floating free.
3. **Evening reflection (the close).** New `FounderOsDailyReflection` model (unique (userId, date), `moved` + `blocked`) via [/api/founder-os/daily-reflections](src/app/api/founder-os/daily-reflections/route.ts) (upsert). `EveningReflectionCard` — the Knapp "reflect" step + Lam 3:40 / Ps 139:23-24. A record, never a verdict.
4. **Time-block the Highlight** (additive `FounderOsDailyGoal.scheduledFor`) + **one-tap "Carry to tomorrow"** (creates tomorrow's open goal respecting its cap, marks today's `carried`).

**Tracking + weekly review.**

5. **Auto-pull into the Sunday review.** [WeeklyThreeExecutionPanel](src/components/founder-hub/founder-os/WeeklyThreeExecutionPanel.tsx) — self-contained (fetches its own data → one import + one mount in the large FounderOSTab), mounted at the TOP of the existing Founder OS weekly-review section. Renders this week's completion + Highlight-hit + the 7-day Sun→Sat strip + Δ vs last week + the week's intentions and whether they landed. Self-hides when there's nothing to show. Uses pure `summarizeWeek` (daily-three.ts).
6. **Discipline → execution correlation.** Pure `computeDisciplineExecutionCorrelation` (daily-three.ts) over the founder's own checkins (SFC-zero) × goal completion. `DisciplineExecutionTile` in the Faith OS tracking area — surfaces "on SFC-zero days you complete X% of your three vs Y% otherwise" only when BOTH buckets clear `MIN_CORRELATION_DAYS` (3); below the floor it shows an honest "keep going" hint, never a fabricated claim.

**Schema:** additive migration [20260601130000_founder_os_period_goals_reflections](prisma/migrations/20260601130000_founder_os_period_goals_reflections/migration.sql) — 2 new tables + 2 nullable columns, zero-risk. **Founder must `npx prisma migrate deploy`** lock-step with deploy (same pattern as every FounderOs\* model). **Gates green:** tsc clean · 35/35 faith-os vitest (20 daily-three incl. summarizeWeek + correlation · 8 period-goals · 7 existing progress) · 4 lints clean (positioning · counts 73 · canonical-imports · silent-catches 217, +5 documented) · prettier · slop-scan 3.23.

**Forward-looking rules (extend the base feature's rules).**

1. **`PERIOD_GOAL_MAX` is locked to `DAILY_THREE_MAX`** — the whole cascade is one Rule of 3; never let them diverge.
2. **Period keys live ONLY in `period-goals.ts`** (`weekKeyFor` / `quarterKeyFor`). Any surface that buckets period goals MUST use them — never inline a week/quarter key (drift-class, same discipline as the canonical-imports lock).
3. **The correlation never renders a claim below `MIN_CORRELATION_DAYS`** — surfacing a base rate off 1-2 days is noise dressed as insight; keep the signal floor.
4. **The cascade link is a SOFT ref** — deleting a period goal must not orphan-crash a daily goal; the UI treats an unresolved `linkedPeriodGoalId` as "no link" (locally unlinks on delete; the server keeps the id harmlessly).
5. **Still no autonomous generation** (rule 3 of the base feature) — weekly/quarterly rocks + the evening reflection are the founder's words; an AI "suggest the week's three" is a founder-routed decision, never a silent ship.

## The Build — Faith OS gamification layer (locked 2026-06-01)

**What it is.** A founder-private gamification/progression layer over the real mission, grounded in Scripture as a business manual. Founder-approved after a gamification-psychology research pass; founder directed the synthesis ("improve consistency / work output / mind, strengthen faith, use the Bible as a business manual"). Mounted at the TOP of the **existing** Start Here tab (the daily landing — NO new tab, per the standing directive). **The customer product (`/dashboard`) is never gamified** — XP on a CSO's decision-audit tool would cheapen the procurement-grade positioning; this is founder-only.

**The load-bearing design rule (why it isn't a dopamine casino).** XP rewards **only controllable INPUTS** — showing up, doing the motion (a DM logged, the three committed, a checkin, a reading). It **never** rewards outcomes you don't control (a reply, a paid conversion, IRR). That single rule satisfies BOTH the Faith OS anti-prosperity guardrail (worth/faithfulness over harvest — "well done, good and faithful servant," Matt 25:21; Prov 16:9) AND the pasted research's core finding (intrinsic motivation compounds when you reward the controllable behavior, not the external result). Outcomes (conversions, retention) drive **milestones + badges**, never XP. No leaderboards (solo founder, N=1 — social comparison doesn't apply). A broken streak is "released," never shame.

**Architecture — derive, don't double-store (NO new tables).** XP / level / quests / milestones / badges all DERIVE from already-logged data, so the points are honest (they reflect real work) and there's zero migration. Pieces:

- **Pure SSOT content** [campaign-content.ts](src/components/founder-hub/campaign/campaign-content.ts) — `XP` rules (inputs only), `LEVEL_ARCS` (7 Scripture builder arcs: Joshua → Nehemiah → Joseph → Daniel → Solomon → Esther → Paul, each carrying a real operating principle), `DAILY_QUESTS` / `WEEKLY_QUESTS` / `CAMPAIGN_MILESTONES` / `BADGES`, and `OPERATING_PRINCIPLES` (the Bible-as-business-manual rotation: Proverbs → work application) + `principleForDate`.
- **Pure engine** [campaign-engine.ts](src/components/founder-hub/campaign/campaign-engine.ts) — `computeCampaign(input)` → XP, level/arc, quest state, milestone progress, badges. 13 vitest ([campaign-engine.test.ts](src/components/founder-hub/campaign/campaign-engine.test.ts)) incl. the **guardrail assertion** that converted/retained never change XP.
- **Aggregation API** [/api/founder-os/campaign](src/app/api/founder-os/campaign/route.ts) — counts/streaks across the FounderOs\* tables (Supabase `user.id`) + the WedgeProspect ledger (literal `userId='founder'`, founder-pass-gated); fails-open to a level-1 campaign on any query error.
- **Cockpit UI** [CampaignCockpit.tsx](src/components/founder-hub/campaign/CampaignCockpit.tsx) — level hero + XP bar + the arc's operating principle + the Proverb-of-the-day + today's/this-week's quests + the campaign milestones (boss-fights) + badges. Self-fetches (reads the public founder-pass env var); mounted at the top of [StartHereTab](src/components/founder-hub/StartHereTab.tsx).

**Gates green:** tsc clean · 13/13 campaign vitest · 4 lints clean (positioning · counts 73 · canonical-imports · silent-catches 218, +1 documented) · prettier · slop-scan 3.24.

**Forward-looking rules.**

1. **XP is inputs-only — permanently.** Any new XP source MUST be a controllable action the founder DOES, never an outcome. The engine test's guardrail assertion (outcomes don't change XP) is the standing shield; extend it when adding XP sources. Outcomes → milestones/badges only.
2. **No leaderboards / social mechanics** — solo founder. Autonomy + mastery + progress + quests + instant feedback are the levers.
3. **Derive from existing data** — never add a parallel points-write on every action (dishonest + a new write path on the hot loop). New signals come from already-logged rows; new tables only with founder approval.
4. **Founder-private only** — never gamify the customer product. When extending, the surfaces are Start Here / Founder OS / Faith OS / Outreach, never `/dashboard`.
5. **Content edits go in `campaign-content.ts`** (XP rules / arcs / quests / milestones / badges / principles); the engine + cockpit read the SSOT. When the GTM motion changes (e.g. the wedge DM target, the kill floor), update the quest/milestone targets there in lockstep with the GTM lock.

## Accountability Sprint tab + server-side founder-hub gate (locked 2026-06-01)

**Founder-hub-internal tab + load-bearing security improvement.** Two related ships landed across the 2026-06-01 commit cluster (commits `0b870fb` → `088ee46`): a new founder-private tab capturing the highest-leverage advisory relationship in the network right now (Kristian Marcus 1-on-1 mentor brief), plus a server-side access gate that closes a real security gap on the entire founder-hub segment.

**Accountability Sprint tab.** A new founder-hub-internal tab in the Go-to-Market cluster. The 4-week startup-accountability sprint collapsed into an exclusive 1-on-1 advisory session (the founder was the only sign-up; the host is travelling in during a tube strike to run it anyway — invested-mentor signal). Kristian Marcus = Product Manager at InsurX (London insurtech, Lloyd's market) — SAME company shape as Decision Intel aimed at a different market: InsurX brings algorithmic discipline to the analog, gut-feel, relationship-driven Lloyd's risk market; DI brings auditable discipline to the analog, gut-feel, relationship-driven M&A / strategy decision market. He has ALREADY solved DI's hardest GTM problem — getting traditional, skeptical institutions to trust an algorithm with decisions they used to make on instinct (40+ Lloyd's brokers + insurers onto InsurX). The brief is the extraction plan. **SSOT** at [sprint-brief-data.ts](src/components/founder-hub/sprint/sprint-brief-data.ts) — `FOUR_WEEK_PLAN` + `EXTRACTION_TARGETS` + `SESSION_LOG` + relationship-play notes; pure-data, no I/O. **Three dynamic vizs** at [SprintVizzes.tsx](src/components/founder-hub/sprint/SprintVizzes.tsx) — `ConvergenceViz` (InsurX↔DI parallel converging on one shape) + `SprintArcViz` (4-week arc with BAFTA T-8d marker in week 1) + `ExtractionLadderViz` (5 ranked extraction targets, A+B as lead). All three are data-driven from the SSOT so they cannot drift from the brief content. Reduced-motion-safe, light-theme-only, CSS-var colours per the locked aesthetic. **Week-1 deliverables** (commit `579d4fd`) — discovery script + leave-behind one-pager so the founder leaves the first session with concrete materials, not just notes. **Tomorrow run sheet** (commit `4851a33`) — literal hours of the first meeting laid out. **Internship-consideration section + refined CV guidance** (commit `9cbc413`) layers the post-mentor career-path discussion WITHOUT leading with it — the prize is the relationship, NOT the internship; the brief carries an explicit caution against the comfort trap (per CLAUDE.md $30M founder cash exit lock — the path to $30M is the wedge, not a US$80K internship). **8 branched questions** (commit `088ee46`) for the 2-3hr session — pre-staged so the founder can read the room and pick the path, not freeze.

**Naming discipline (load-bearing).** The TAB LABEL is role-neutral `Accountability Sprint` per the CLAUDE.md no-named-prospects rule for the shipped bundle; the brief CONTENT names Kristian / InsurX exactly like the LRQA / Cornerstone briefs name their subjects internally. He is a personal mentor, not a confidential prospect, but the label stays event-based for audit-safety + consistency. The same rule that protected `lrqa` + `cornerstone` from public-surface leak protects `accountability_sprint`.

**AccentCard discipline.** The surface uses AccentCard extensively (info / warning / primary / danger accents per section role per the CLAUDE.md AccentCard primitive lock). Two `color: '#fff'` literals at line 422 + 698 are on small colored badge backgrounds (white-on-color contrast pattern, NOT dark-mode drift) — they are intentional and tolerated.

**Server-side founder-hub access gate (commit `5a6205a`).** New [src/app/(platform)/dashboard/founder-hub/layout.tsx](<src/app/(platform)/dashboard/founder-hub/layout.tsx>) is a 63-line async server component that gates the ENTIRE founder-hub segment server-side via `isAdminUserId()` BEFORE the page or any nested brief renders. Before this ship the hub was protected ONLY by (a) Supabase platform auth (any logged-in user reached the page) + (b) a CLIENT-SIDE password compared against `NEXT_PUBLIC_FOUNDER_HUB_PASS` (the public var inlines into the JS bundle that ships to every browser — anyone authed could read the pass out of the bundle, bypass the client gate, and see founder-only content including positioning strategy, prospect briefs, mentor brief, exit math). **SAFE-BY-DEFAULT** — when `ADMIN_USER_IDS` is unset (e.g. before the founder bootstraps the env var via `/api/admin/whoami`) the layout falls through to the existing client password gate so the founder is NEVER locked out of their own hub. The hard gate ACTIVATES the moment `ADMIN_USER_IDS` is set in Vercel; until then current behaviour is preserved. The client password gate stays as defense-in-depth (e.g. a borrowed-but-logged-in session on the founder's own machine). Bootstrap: set `ADMIN_EMAILS` first, deploy, hit `/api/admin/whoami` while logged in to get the Supabase UUID, paste into `ADMIN_USER_IDS`, redeploy.

**Residual exposure (honest disclosure).** Next.js client chunks are inherently inspectable, so true zero-leak of founder-hub content would require server-only rendering of every hub-tab body (a larger rearchitecture). For the current stage the route gate (non-founders get redirected; the page + its dynamic chunks are NEVER served to them) is the proportionate fix.

**Forward-looking rules.**

1. **When a new founder-hub-internal brief / tab lands** (Sankore / LRQA / Cornerstone / Accountability Sprint pattern), the server gate above protects it automatically — NEVER re-implement page-level auth; the segment-level `layout.tsx` is the single point. The auth posture you need is already inherited.
2. **The Accountability Sprint brief is LIVING** — after every weekly session, update `SESSION_LOG` + the relationship-play notes in [sprint-brief-data.ts](src/components/founder-hub/sprint/sprint-brief-data.ts). The vizs read from the SSOT and update automatically.
3. **Strategy stays locked to the GTM motion** — Kristian is a mentor, NOT a Phase 1 wedge persona. The discipline that prevents asking him for a sale OR positioning DI to him as an enterprise pilot is documented in the brief's caution sections. Never let a future ship drift the brief into "Kristian as buyer."
4. **The naming-discipline pattern (role-neutral tab label + named-subject brief content) is the canonical shape for every future personal-relationship founder-hub brief**. New brief targeted at a named individual? Tab id is event-shaped (`mentor_brief_X` / `advisory_brief_X` / `partnership_brief_X`), brief content names the subject internally, no name leaks to the production bundle. Same pattern as LRQA + Cornerstone + Accountability Sprint.
5. **The "naming-discipline pattern" applies to comments too** — keep source-code JSDoc / `//` comments role-neutral if they reference a current prospect. SWC strips them at prod build, but the source-discipline survives audits and git-log searches.

## SAT Prep — founder-private study surface (locked 2026-06-07)

**What it is.** A founder-private SAT study system in the founder-hub (`sat_prep` tab, Foundations cluster, next to Faith OS). Founder-directed build after the founder pushed back on the anti-build framing ("you keep forgetting how efficient you are — the full build can be done in an afternoon"); his own Velocity & Scope Discipline lock backs that ("don't pre-shrink"). **The customer product (`/dashboard`) is NEVER touched** — this is single-user, founder-pass-gated, partitioned by Supabase user.id like every FounderOs\* surface. **FOUNDER ACTION: `npx prisma migrate deploy` lock-step with the deploy** (migration `20260607120000_sat_prep` — 4 new additive tables only, zero-risk; pre-migration the routes fail-soft to empty).

**The numbers + strategy (SSOT in [sat-content.ts](src/components/founder-hub/sat/sat-content.ts) `SAT_GOAL`):** 1280 PSAT → 1550 target · 30 min/day · September benchmark → November target. Math-to-ceiling-then-R&W (Math is the trainable + founder's edge). The load-bearing honest facts (`SAT_STRATEGIC_NOTES`): **UC Berkeley is test-blind** (this effort is for Stanford + test-requiring privates, NOT Berkeley); Stanford superscores (Sept + Nov); the digital SAT is adaptive (only official scoring is truth); vocab is de-emphasised.

**The load-bearing architecture rule — source-of-truth split (do NOT blur):** official Bluebook/Khan/released tests are the SOLE source of the projected score (`SatTestResult` → `computeProjectedScore`). AI-generated drills (`/api/founder-os/sat/generate`, `MODEL_CHEAP` + mock fallback) are for targeted reps on a DIAGNOSED weak skill ONLY — off-distribution at the 1550 ceiling, so they never feed the score. This split is enforced in the data model + must stay enforced.

**The calibration loop (the Decision-Intel lens applied to the test-taker):** every drill question is confidence-tagged (0-3) BEFORE answering; `computeCalibration` Brier-scores the confidence-vs-correctness gap (N-floor `CALIBRATION_MIN_N=5`, same honesty as Vohra). `overconfidentMisses` (confidence ≥2 but wrong) is the highest-ROI review list — a baited System-1 pattern. XP rewards INPUTS only (reps + showing up), never the score — same anti-prosperity discipline as the campaign layer.

**Files.** Pure SSOT [sat-content.ts](src/components/founder-hub/sat/sat-content.ts) (skill taxonomy = digital-SAT domains, root causes, score targets, XP, study-plan phases) + pure tested math [sat-calibration.ts](src/components/founder-hub/sat/sat-calibration.ts) (Brier / weak-area / projected-score / streak, 20 vitest) · 4 Prisma models (`SatErrorLogEntry` the heart + `SatDailySession` + `SatTestResult` + `SatVocabCard`) · 5 routes under [/api/founder-os/sat/](src/app/api/founder-os/sat) (error-log · sessions · tests · vocab · generate — all `authenticateFounderOs` + fail-soft) · shell [SatPrepTab.tsx](src/components/founder-hub/SatPrepTab.tsx) + 4 surfaces in [sat/](src/components/founder-hub/sat) (Daily Training · Official Test Log · Progress & Calibration · Vocab Bank) · vocab reuses the Education Room `applySm2` engine (one home for SM-2) · companion plan [docs/sat-study-plan.md](docs/sat-study-plan.md).

**Gates green at ship:** tsc clean (0 non-e2e errors) · 20/20 sat-calibration vitest · 4 lints (positioning · counts 73 · canonical-imports · silent-catches 218→226, +8 documented canonical body-parse/fire-and-forget class) · prettier · slop-scan 3.26.

**Forward-looking rules.** (1) **The source-of-truth split is permanent** — AI-generated content NEVER feeds the projected score; only `SatTestResult` does. (2) **XP is inputs-only** — never reward a score or a test result. (3) **Score/skill/plan edits go in `sat-content.ts`**; the calibration math lives ONLY in `sat-calibration.ts` (never re-implement Brier/weak-area inline). (4) **Founder-private only** — never surface SAT on `/dashboard` or any customer page; the founder-hub server gate protects it automatically. (5) **No autonomous content as truth** — drills are practice; the founder logs real tests + real misses; never auto-infer a score.

### SAT Prep v2 — all-improvements boil-the-ocean (locked 2026-06-07, same day, founder "boil the ocean, goal is consistency + 1550")

Four bundles shipped in one autonomous session (3 incremental commits, all gates green). **FOUNDER ACTION: a 2nd migration — `npx prisma migrate deploy` picks up both `20260607120000_sat_prep` + `20260607130000_sat_prep_v2`** (SM-2 review columns + cached `explanation` on `SatErrorLogEntry` + `SatSettings`; additive, zero-risk).

1. **Active error loop (the pedagogical core).** Each logged MISS (`wasCorrect=false`) is scheduled for SM-2 spaced review (`nextDue` set at create; correct attempts stay calibration substrate only). New **Review** tab (5th surface, [SatReview.tsx](src/components/founder-hub/sat/SatReview.tsx)) — recall before reveal (retrieval > re-reading; Roediger & Karpicke), self-grade Again/Hard/Good/Easy → `applySm2` reschedules; auto-retires at interval ≥21d. **"Explain this miss"** tutor ([/api/founder-os/sat/explain](src/app/api/founder-os/sat/explain/route.ts), `MODEL_FOUNDER_HUB` Grok, caches on the row, mock fallback) — operates on the founder's OWN logged miss, never fabricates a question. The error-log PATCH gained `reviewQuality` (SM-2) + `reviewArchived`.
2. **Real-test miss capture.** Test Log gained a per-skill tap grid (`source='official_test'`) so weak-area ranking + the Brier loop are built on REAL Bluebook questions, not just off-distribution AI drills (the correctness gap in v1).
3. **Per-skill calibration + Brier trend.** `computeCalibrationBySkill` + `computeCalibrationTrend` (weekly Sunday-bucket Brier) + `daysUntil` + `isDueForReview` (+9 vitest, **29 total**). Surfaced in Progress (per-skill gaps + an SVG `Sparkline`).
4. **Consistency engine (the #1 goal).** Test-date countdown strip (T-minus to Sept benchmark + Nov target; editable, persisted to `SatSettings`; defaults in `SAT_TEST_DATE_DEFAULTS` — editable, NOT a hardcoded College Board claim). SAT wired into **The Build campaign as INPUTS-ONLY XP** (`satSession` + `satRep` in `XP`/`CampaignCounts`/`computeXp`; aggregated via a separate Promise.all in the campaign route to avoid the aligned-destructure risk; guardrail test extended — outcomes still never change XP). Cross-surface [SatReminderCard](src/components/founder-hub/sat/SatReminderCard.tsx) on Start Here (streak + due-count + countdown, framed as a Gollwitzer implementation intention; self-hides when empty). `SAT_LEARNING_SCIENCE` SSOT names the 6 anchors (retrieval, spacing, interleaving, calibration, implementation intentions, desirable difficulties).

**Deliberately DEFERRED (recorded boundaries, founder-gated — NOT silent omissions):** (a) **per-question drill timing** — a Tier-3 nicety; the `timing` root-cause tag already captures pacing qualitatively, and a live per-question timer + "you're slow on X" analytic is a drill-flow change better validated with an eyeball (no browser in the build sandbox). (b) **cron email nudge** — outward-send infra (founder's own inbox, but still a scheduled send that can become noise); the in-product `SatReminderCard` on the daily-landing Start Here is the higher-leverage, zero-infra consistency surface. Both are clean follow-ups, not gaps. (c) the full **voice "SAT tutor" thinking-partner persona** — "Explain this miss" delivers the tutor value in-tab; a voice-worker persona is a separate integration.

**Forward-looking (extends the base rules):** SM-2 over misses reuses `applySm2` (one home — never fork the algorithm); the active loop must drive MORE official practice + review, never become a thing to keep building (the displacement guardrail); any new XP source stays inputs-only (the campaign guardrail test is the shield).

### SAT Prep v3 — vocab engine (locked 2026-06-07, founder "fix low-level words + sloppy SR + tie in my old Forge/WordForge features"; founder-scoped via AskUserQuestion: full adaptive engine, MindForge skipped)

The Vocab Bank was producing mid-level common words (underscore/mitigate/pragmatic) on a plain flip-reveal — useless at the 1550 ceiling. This ship made the (deliberately THIN) vocab slice genuinely excellent by porting the GOOD parts of the founder's prior Forge/WordForge system. **FOUNDER ACTION: a 3rd SAT migration — `npx prisma migrate deploy` now picks up `20260607120000_sat_prep` + `20260607130000_sat_prep_v2` + `20260607140000_sat_vocab_engine`** (additive substrate + SR-richness columns on `SatVocabCard`; zero-risk).

1. **Word quality (the "underscore" fix).** [generate/route.ts](src/app/api/founder-os/sat/generate/route.ts) now has a hard difficulty floor + easy-word exclusion + dedup against the founder's existing words, all sourced from the new `SAT_VOCAB_GEN` SSOT in [sat-content.ts](src/components/founder-hub/sat/sat-content.ts) (`tooEasyExamples` + `targetExamples`). The mock fallback was upgraded from one word to four hard, full-substrate words, so the surface is good even with no API key.
2. **Honest SR (the "sloppy" fix) — WITHOUT forking `applySm2`.** The shared engine stays the one home; the fix is a pure `effectiveQuality({correct, confidence, responseMs})` in [sat-calibration.ts](src/components/founder-hub/sat/sat-calibration.ts) that computes a smarter SM-2 quality INPUT (wrong+confident → 0, the baited System-1 miss; correct+unsure → 3, don't over-extend; certain+correct → 5; fast→+1 cap 5, slow→−1 floored at 3 so a correct answer never resets the streak) then feeds the unchanged `applySm2`. Plus per-card response-time EMA (`updateResponseMsEma`) + per-quiz-type failure memory (`nextFailedTypes`) + `consecutiveFailures`. This IS the calibration loop applied to scheduling — the system's own thesis, finally wired into vocab. 15 new vitest (44 total).
3. **Multi-type adaptive review** ([SatVocabReview.tsx](src/components/founder-hub/sat/SatVocabReview.tsx)) — the SAT-relevant subset only (NOT Forge's 12-type kitchen sink): **context cloze** (the most test-aligned, since the SAT tests words IN CONTEXT), definition both directions, synonyms, antonyms. `pickAdaptiveQuizType` targets a card's weak angle (its `failedTypes`); confidence is tagged before answering; response time is captured; distractors are sampled from the collection (no per-word distractor generation, no extra schema); cloze derives from the stored `clozeSentence` or the example sentence. Graceful fallback to recall-before-reveal when there are <4 cards or no substrate.
4. **Richer cards** ([SatVocabBank.tsx](src/components/founder-hub/sat/SatVocabBank.tsx)) — IPA, etymology, synonym/antonym/related chips, the founder's OWN-mnemonic input (the generation effect — self-made aids stick harder; saved via a new mnemonic POST branch) + the AI mnemonic hidden behind "Reveal AI hint" (try yourself first).

**Deliberately NOT ported (recorded boundaries, founder-confirmed — not silent omissions):** (a) **MindForge** (Argument Builder / Analogy / Summary / Impromptu Speaking) — off-target for SAT-1550 (the digital SAT R&W tests reading comprehension + grammar, not argument construction or speech); the founder's comms training already lives in the Sparring Room + Education Room. (b) **The Forge RPG combat economy** (boss-damage, gold, combat math) — the SAT system is inputs-only XP via The Build campaign (anti-prosperity lock); combat math would violate it. (c) **The knowledge-graph nodes** — a different system.

**Gates green:** tsc clean (0 non-e2e) · 44/44 sat-calibration vitest · 5 lints (positioning · counts 73 · canonical-imports · silent-catches 231 unchanged — the removed flip-reveal catch offset the new ones · doc-sync) · prettier · slop-scan.

**Forward-looking rules.** (1) **Vocab stays THIN in the daily plan** — this ship made the slice excellent, NOT bigger; never let vocab grow into a dominant time-share (the digital SAT de-emphasises rare-word recall). (2) **Never fork `applySm2`** — confidence/speed shape the quality INPUT, not the algorithm. (3) A new review type ⇒ extend `SAT_VOCAB_QUIZ_TYPES` + the `buildQuestion` eligibility/builder + a test, in lockstep. (4) Distractors are sampled from the collection — never auto-generate per-word distractors (cost + schema bloat). (5) XP stays inputs-only; the score still comes ONLY from `SatTestResult` (the source-of-truth split is untouched). (6) MindForge stays out of the SAT tool — if the founder ever wants a standalone thinking-gym, that's its own surface, separate from test prep.

## Founder Hub brain-dump intake (locked 2026-06-07, founder "boil the ocean" — friction-killer for tab/field sprawl)

**What it is.** A `DailyDumpPanel` on Start Here (the daily landing): the founder dumps his whole day in one free-form blurb (dictate with **Wispr Flow** → paste — no new audio infra), and an AI extracts a batch of PROPOSED log actions across the founder-os surfaces; he confirms / edits / drops / picks; the client then writes the confirmed ones to the EXISTING endpoints. Kills the "open six tabs, fill six forms" friction that was leaving the ledgers empty — which the founder's own execution-discipline lock flags as the displacement signal.

**THE load-bearing rule — CONFIRM-BEFORE-WRITE, never silent autonomous.** The parse endpoint writes NOTHING; it only proposes. The ledgers this feeds (the conversion ledger → month-4 kill checkpoint, the Vohra cohort, the campaign) are too load-bearing to accept a silent misparse — a phantom prospect or a wrongly-completed goal corrupts the exact signals the strategy is scored on. So: dump → propose → **one glance to confirm** → batch-write. Ambiguous entity references (which goal? which prospect?) are flagged `needsPick` with candidates, never guessed. This is the same discipline as every "no autonomous fabrication" lock in the codebase.

**Architecture.** SSOT [intake-actions.ts](src/lib/founder-hub/intake/intake-actions.ts) — 8 action types + `INTAKE_ACTION_META` (per-type `fields` [drives BOTH the LLM's expected output AND the generic review card], `icon`/`accent`, `summarize`, and **`toRequest` — the ONLY place that maps an action → existing endpoint + body**). Pure [intake-parse.ts](src/lib/founder-hub/intake/intake-parse.ts) — `normalizeIntakeActions` (validate type, coerce fields per kind, drop unknowns) + `matchByName` entity-match + `resolvePick` + `isActionReady` (15 vitest). Endpoint [/api/founder-hub/intake/parse](src/app/api/founder-hub/intake/parse/route.ts) — ONE `MODEL_FOUNDER_HUB` (Grok) call at temp 0.2, the catalog + rules derived from the SSOT so the prompt can't drift, `authenticateFounderOs`, mock-empty fallback when no key. UI [DailyDumpPanel](src/components/founder-hub/intake/DailyDumpPanel.tsx) — self-contained (env founder-pass, like CampaignCockpit/SatReminderCard), fetches context (today's open goals + active prospects for matching), generic review card renders ANY action type from its `FieldSpec[]`, and the **client executor dispatches each confirmed action to the EXISTING write endpoint** (reuses their validation + audit-log + fail-soft — no parallel server-side write path, zero duplication).

**The 18 daily-fill action types, in 5 review clusters** (8 → 15 → 18 over 2026-06-07; NOT all ~40 founder write endpoints — scoped to what the founder actually dumps): **Goals & day** — `daily_goal` · `complete_goal` (matches an open goal) · `period_goal` (week/quarter rock) · `commitment` · `daily_reflection` · `weekly_review` (weekly, emitted only on an explicit week review). **Work & follow-ups** — `meeting_log` · `todo_add` · `todo_complete` (matches an open to-do). **Outreach** — `prospect_create` · `prospect_advance` (matches an active prospect). **Faith OS** — `faith_checkin` · `prayer_journal` · `reading_progress`. **Learning** — `sat_session` · `sat_test` (scored full-length) · `content_log` (a learning takeaway) · `skill_dev` (quarterly skill goal). Each maps to exactly one existing route. **Deliberately excluded** (recorded, not silent): `sat/error-log` (entries need the specific question to seed the review loop — better logged in the SAT tab; a dump miss = a degraded review card), outreach artifacts / design-partner contacts / content-studio generation (not daily logs), `faith-companion` (a chat, not a log).

**On merging actions (the founder asked).** Action TYPES are deliberately NOT merged into multi-write super-actions — each action = exactly one endpoint, so confirm/edit/drop + per-action result reporting stays honest (no partial-write ambiguity, and the executor can reuse each route's own validation/audit). The compression that actually helps at scale is two non-type-merging moves, both shipped: (1) **review-UX grouping** — proposed actions render grouped by `cluster` (the `INTAKE_CLUSTERS` SSOT), so a 10-action dump reads as 5 tidy sections, not a flat wall; (2) **parse rules that avoid double-logging the same fact** — the prompt instructs: a bare "prayed / read scripture" → ONE `faith_checkin` (booleans), and `prayer_journal`/`reading_progress` only when there's specific content; a study session → `sat_session`, a scored full-length → `sat_test`, a reading takeaway → `content_log`. So "compression" lives in the parse + the grouping, never in collapsing the endpoint mapping.

**No schema change** (reuses existing tables/endpoints/auth). **No new audio infra** — Wispr-paste is the voice path; the LiveKit voice worker + `voice-tools` route stay as a future richer in-app-voice option, deliberately not the v1.

**Gates green:** tsc clean (0 non-e2e) · eslint clean · 21/21 intake vitest · 5 lints (positioning · counts 73 · canonical-imports · silent-catches 236 [+5 documented canonical body-parse] · doc-sync) · prettier · slop-scan under 4.0.

**Forward-looking rules.** (1) **Add an action = add to `IntakeActionType` + `INTAKE_ACTION_META`** (with `fields` + `cluster` + `toRequest`; a target-bound action also adds a one-line entry to `TARGET_SOURCES` in intake-parse.ts) + extend the parse test — the parser, review card (grouped by `cluster`), and executor all read the SSOT, so that's the whole cascade. (Now at 18 actions across 5 clusters.) `isActionReady` requires EVERY non-optional field (not just the primary) so multi-required actions like `weekly_review` / `content_log` gate correctly. (2) **Confirm-before-write is permanent** — never add a silent autonomous mass-writer near the ledgers; the review gate IS the integrity guarantee. (3) **The executor dispatches to existing endpoints** — never build a parallel server-side write path that re-implements their validation/audit. (4) **Entity ambiguity → `needsPick`, never a guessed `targetId`.** (5) Founder-private only (Start Here); the server founder-hub gate protects it. (6) Wispr-paste stays the voice path unless the founder explicitly asks to wire the in-app voice worker.

## Argument Builder — the one MindForge principle, ported into the Sparring Room (locked 2026-06-07)

**What it is.** A **Claim → Evidence → Counterargument → Rebuttal** reasoning drill — a second surface inside the Sparring Room (a `surface` toggle: "Live reps" | "Argument Builder"). The founder states a claim, evidences it, **steelmans** the strongest objection, then rebuts it; an LLM grades it. It trains structured reasoning for investor-Q&A / pitch defence — the founder's real need before Strategy World / VC diligence.

**Why ONLY this principle (the honest scoping).** A close read found ~most of MindForge already lives in DI: rubric grading + model exemplar (the Sparring Room), try-before-reveal / generation effect (SAT vocab + Education recall), XP/streaks (The Build), data cross-pollination (FOUNDER_CONTEXT). Porting the whole gym would be exactly the tab/feature sprawl the founder just asked to fight. The Claim→Evidence→Counter→Rebuttal scaffold was the one genuinely additive piece, and it folds into an existing surface (no new tab) reusing the Sparring grader infra. Analogy Engine + Summary Challenge were judged lower-leverage and NOT built (recorded).

**Architecture.** Pure SSOT + logic [argument-builder.ts](src/components/founder-hub/sparring/argument-builder.ts) — 5 claim categories (investor_objection / moat_defense / category_claim / strategic_decision / bring_your_own, seeded with the founder's real context), the 4-part scaffold, the 4-dim rubric (clarity / logic / evidence / rebuttal-strength), `argumentReadiness` (all four parts required to grade — the scaffold IS the lesson), `normalizeArgumentResult` (clamps the LLM grade, never throws), `mockArgumentResult` (honest no-key fallback — overall 0, not a fake score), 7 vitest. Endpoint [/api/founder-hub/argument-builder](src/app/api/founder-hub/argument-builder/route.ts) — two actions (`generate` a debatable claim · `grade` the 4-part argument), `MODEL_FOUNDER_HUB` (Grok), `verifyFounderPass`, mock fallback. UI [ArgumentBuilder.tsx](src/components/founder-hub/sparring/ArgumentBuilder.tsx) — category picker + generate-a-claim + the 4 fields + a result card (0-100 + 4 sub-score bars + a **steelman verdict** [steelman / weak / strawman, the most common failure] + strengths/improvements + an expert model-answer) + a localStorage score-trend. Mounted in [SparringRoomTab](src/components/founder-hub/SparringRoomTab.tsx) via the surface toggle (early-return for the argument surface; the live-rep flow is untouched).

**The grader's load-bearing bias:** it is hardest on a **weak counterargument** — a strawman the author can knock down trivially. The prompt + the `steelmanVerdict` make "did you steelman the real objection?" the headline signal, because that's the exact failure that loses an investor room.

**Gates green:** tsc + eslint clean · 7/7 argument vitest · 5 lints (positioning · counts 73 · canonical-imports · silent-catches 238 [+2 documented body-parse] · doc-sync) · prettier · slop-scan under 4.0. No schema change.

**Forward-looking rules.** (1) The drill lives in the Sparring Room, not a new tab — if a future MindForge principle is ported, fold it into an existing surface, never spawn a gym (the anti-sprawl rule the founder set). (2) A new claim category = add to `ARGUMENT_CATEGORIES` + `ARGUMENT_SEED_CLAIMS` + the endpoint's `CATEGORY_PROMPT` in lockstep. (3) `normalizeArgumentResult` is the only place that trusts the LLM grade — keep it total (clamp, default, never throw). (4) Analogy Engine / Summary Challenge stay UN-built unless the founder asks; they were evaluated lower-leverage.

## 66-Day Protocol — founder-private "choose reality" tracker (locked 2026-06-14)

**What it is.** A new founder-hub tab (`reality_protocol`, Foundations cluster, sibling to Faith OS) — the personal operating plan from `docs/66-day-protocol.md` made into a daily ritual. Two ~15-second check-ins a day (a morning intention + a night honest mark) grow a tree to full bloom at day 66 (Start 14 Jun → Finish 19 Aug 2026, the day school resumes). Founder-directed build. The customer product (`/dashboard`) is NEVER touched; single-user, founder-pass-gated, partitioned by Supabase user.id like every other `FounderOs*` surface, and inherits the server-side founder-hub admin gate automatically. **FOUNDER ACTION: `npx prisma migrate deploy`** lock-step with deploy — migration `20260614120000_founder_os_reality_protocol` (one additive table, zero-risk; pre-migration the route fails soft to an empty seed).

**On putting it in the codebase (the prior-AI objection, addressed not ignored).** The ChatGPT/Claude threads that designed this argued *against* wiring it into Decision Intel (avoidance-in-disguise + private-data-hygiene). The founder weighed that and chose the Founder Hub anyway, and it's the right home: the hub is already server-gated to admin-only (`isAdminUserId()`) and already holds the most private founder data (Faith OS prayer journal, spiritual check-ins, exit math). A 66-day tracker is a natural Faith OS sibling; the hygiene concern is addressed by that existing isolation (founder-scoped table, founder-pass + Supabase dual gate), not a new exposure. The DI *commercial* data the prior AI worried about is a different surface.

**The LOAD-BEARING invariants (the whole design — encoded in code, not just copy).** (1) The tree grows from SHOWING UP (check-ins), never from elapsed calendar time, and a slip is a check-in like any other — so a slip night still GROWS the tree. (2) A slip is logged honestly but NEVER resets the tree or progress — there is NO streak counter (the abstinence-violation trap "the day's ruined, what's the point" is the real enemy; a reset-counter manufactures it). (3) Exactly ONE morning question + ONE night mark — no six-factor "reality score", no Prince/King second timeline, no in-app AI (all explicitly CUT in the design thread; at the urge moment you want fewer screens + a faster action, not a conversation). (4) Day 66 = graduation; the tool is built to retire. The pure test suite (`tree-growth.test.ts`, 16 vitest) locks invariants 1+2 directly ("a slip GROWS the tree, never resets it"; "progress only ever increases").

**Architecture (mirrors Faith OS / FounderOs\* exactly).** Pure SSOT [content.ts](src/components/founder-hub/reality-protocol/content.ts) (dates + cadence + the morning question + KJV verse pool + RISING_VERSE_REFS for slip nights + the 4 keystones + anti-goal + research note + tree stages) · pure math [tree-growth.ts](src/components/founder-hub/reality-protocol/tree-growth.ts) (`computeProtocolState` / `checkinsForDay` / `selectVerse` / `finishIso`; `progress = min(1, totalCheckins / CHECKINS_TO_BLOOM)` where CHECKINS_TO_BLOOM = 66×2) · 16 vitest · Prisma model `FounderOsRealityCheckin` (one row per `(userId, date, kind)`, upserted; `escapePlan` morning, `stayedOnTrack` night) · route [/api/founder-os/reality-checkin](src/app/api/founder-os/reality-checkin/route.ts) (GET/POST-upsert/DELETE-reset, `authenticateFounderOs`, `@schema-drift-tolerant` fail-soft) · UI [RealityProtocolTab.tsx](src/components/founder-hub/RealityProtocolTab.tsx) (platform-token cards) + the immersive sky+tree hero [RealityTree.tsx](src/components/founder-hub/reality-protocol/RealityTree.tsx) (self-contained `intentional-dark` SVG illustration with its own palette — the one rich-palette carve-out, like the viz/DPR surfaces; reduced-motion-safe). 4-table lockstep done: TabId union + TABS + TAB_CONTENT + SEARCH_INDEX in the hub page · `chat-nav.ts` TAB_NAV_TARGETS · founder-context `[[nav]]` list.

**Gates green:** tsc clean (0 non-e2e) · 19/19 reality-protocol vitest · eslint clean · lints at baseline (positioning · counts 73 · canonical-imports · **silent-catches 238 unchanged** — the fetch consumers use try/catch-with-comment + direct `res.json()`, no new `.catch(() => null)`) · prettier · audit-platform 0 CRITICAL/MODAL/STALE/SEMANTIC · slop-scan < 4.0.

**Follow-up (2026-06-14, same day — founder-requested polish + the prod table fix).** (a) **Night/morning-mark undo** — `editingMorning`/`editingNight` state + a "Change" link on the done-box reopens the day's mark (the upsert overwrites), fixing a mis-tap with no escape but reset. (b) **Mobile stack** — the side-by-side action pairs get `.reality-night-actions` + a `@media (max-width:420px)` column stack. (c) **The Einstein line** — `INSANITY_QUOTE` ("Insanity is doing the same thing over and over again and expecting different results.") shown as a quiet standing motto; attributed "attributed to Albert Einstein" (the attribution is apocryphal — the honest hedge mirrors the 21-day-myth note). (d) **Context surfaced** — the bottom section is now "The diagnosis, the loop & the plan" (default-OPEN; the check-in stays above it so the ritual isn't slowed): `DIAGNOSIS_REFRAME` (the "same muscle" frame) + the **dynamic loop viz** ([LoopViz.tsx](src/components/founder-hub/reality-protocol/LoopViz.tsx) — the 7-stage escape cycle as an orbiting ring, token-driven + reduced-motion-safe, with the phone/feed on-ramp highlighted as the leverage point "cut here") + the 4 keystones + `CONSTRUCTION_SWAPS` (pre-decided escape→construction list) + anti-goal + research note. 3 new LOOP_STAGES invariant tests (19 total). (e) **Build OOM fix** — the build's `tsc --noEmit` step was pinned at `--max-old-space-size=3584` and the codebase's tsc working set had crept to that ceiling (a real build hit ~3536 MB → "ineffective mark-compacts near heap limit"); bumped to **6144** (safe: tsc runs as its own process and exits before `next build`'s 7168 webpack step, sequential `&&`, so peak is unchanged). (f) **Pre-existing SVG bug swept** — `FounderHubMap.tsx` + `SprintVizzes.tsx` used the invalid `height="auto"` SVG *attribute* (→ "Expected length, auto" console error); moved to `style={{ height: 'auto' }}` (valid CSS). NOT from this feature — LoopViz/RealityTree use the valid style form.

**PROD TABLE NOTE (load-bearing).** The build's `prisma-migrate-safe` step hit **P1001 — direct `:5432` unreachable** (Supabase direct connection paused/restricted on Hobby), so the migration did NOT auto-apply; the app reaches the DB fine at runtime via the pooler, so GET fails soft (empty seed) but the POST upsert 500s ("table does not exist"). Fix path when direct conn is down: apply the additive table via the Supabase **SQL Editor** (or the Supabase MCP `apply_migration`, which needs founder approval) — the migration SQL + the `_prisma_migrations` bookkeeping row (checksum `c20ec945…`) keep Prisma in sync so a later `migrate deploy` skips it. **Any other migration dated after the last successful `migrate deploy` is in the same boat** (analysis-quota 06-06, SAT 06-07) — verify/apply those too once direct conn is restored.

**Forward-looking rules.** (1) The invariants above are the point — never add a streak counter, never let a slip reduce `progress`, never add a second tracked input or an in-app AI. (2) The verse pool is KJV by deliberate choice (the slip anchor Prov 24:16 is quoted KJV throughout the plan); edit verses in `content.ts` only. (3) `PROTOCOL_START_ISO` + `PROTOCOL_TOTAL_DAYS` are the SSOT — the finish date + bloom target derive; never hardcode "Aug 19" or "132". (4) Founder-private only — never surface on `/dashboard` or any customer page; the founder-hub server gate protects it automatically. (5) The tab is built to RETIRE at day 66 — if the founder asks to wind it down, that's expected, not a regression. (6) The LoopViz assumes exactly ONE leverage stage (the test locks it) — when editing `LOOP_STAGES`, keep a single `leverage: true`.
