+ `buildOrgRoiSummary` which COMPOSES the canonical `getQuarterlyImpact` + `getOrgBrierStats` + `PLATFORM_BASELINE_SNAPSHOT`, never recomputing them, with honest `unlocks → emerging → live` calibration bands ≥5 outcomes mirroring the Vohra N-floor) + 14 vitest; route [/api/analytics/roi](src/app/api/analytics/roi/route.ts) (mirrors the flywheel auth/org-resolve, schema-drift-tolerant); [OrgRoiCard](src/components/outcome-flywheel/OrgRoiCard.tsx) mounted as the LEAD of [OutcomeFlywheelContent](src/components/outcome-flywheel/OutcomeFlywheelContent.tsx) — the exact surface the audit named "renders metrics, never a value narrative". **#3** — a non-gated loop-close banner in [InlineAnalysisResultCard](src/components/analysis/InlineAnalysisResultCard.tsx) at the post-upload reveal, routed to the Deep Dive where the outcome reporter already lives (feeds #2's calibration data). **Honesty is procurement-grade and lives in the SSOT**: value-at-stake is a flag of EXPOSURE the audit surfaced (anchored to the ticket the user entered), explicitly NOT a prediction of loss; decisions with a ticket but no flagged-pattern cohort are excluded, never invented; the calibration delta is never shown as "sharpened" below N=5. **Recorded scope boundaries (deliberate, not dangling threads):** a main-`/dashboard` ROI teaser (the dashboard is a 2,870-line monolith + grep tooling was unreliable on it — the Outcome Flywheel is the purpose-built retention page and the correct single home; a teaser is additive) and unifying the Flywheel's existing `quarterlyImpact` block to read the same SSOT (it already shows `estimatedSavings` via its own route; OrgRoiCard leads the page so the value narrative is present — full consolidation is a separate ship). **Forward rule:** the value math lives ONLY in `decision-roi.ts`; never recompute `getQuarterlyImpact`/`getOrgBrierStats` — compose them (same drift-class discipline as the canonical-imports lock).

- **Friction audit #4 — non-fatal enrichment must NEVER block the audit critical path (locked 2026-05-17).** Friction #1 (demo SSE, real progress, fake-cycler removed) surfaced a **platform-wide P0**, not a demo bug: [contextBuilder.ts](src/lib/intelligence/contextBuilder.ts) `ensureFreshNews()` did `await utilTimeout(() => syncAllFeeds(), 60_000, …)` **sequentially before** the parallel intelligence fan-out, and `assembleContext` is called by the pipeline's `intelligenceGatherer` node ([nodes.ts:488](src/lib/agents/nodes.ts#L488)) — the SAME pipeline `analyzeDocument` (demo) AND every authed [/api/analyze/stream](src/app/api/analyze/stream/route.ts) run. On any cold/>12h-stale-DB process the audit froze ~60s at the intelligence phase platform-wide; the fake progress cycler had masked it, so removing it (friction #1) correctly exposed the real hang (grep-proven via the user's own `[ContextBuilder] On-demand news sync … timeout` terminal log, not theory). **Fix A** — news is non-fatal prompt enrichment; the daily cron is the real refresh, `ensureFreshNews` is only a between-crons safety net. The on-demand sync is now backgrounded: `syncAllFeeds().catch(log.warn)` raced against `sleep(ON_DEMAND_NEWS_MAX_WAIT_MS = 5_000)` — a fast sync still benefits this audit, otherwise it proceeds immediately with cached news while the sync keeps running in the background (`Promise.race` does NOT cancel it; its writes land for subsequent audits within the process). 60s critical-path block → ≤5s. **Fix B** — exported pure `parseFeedDate()` ([newsService.ts](src/lib/news/newsService.ts)) guards the FCA-class unparseable pubDate that resolved to `Invalid Date`, threw inside the Prisma upsert (`Invalid value for argument publishedAt`) and crash-spammed a full object per article, serially slowing the sync. 5-test regression lock at [newsService.test.ts](src/lib/news/newsService.test.ts). **Speed C/D** — the formerly-sequential Gemini classification (11 batches one-at-a-time) and article upserts (210 one-at-a-time DB round-trips) now run through the canonical `batchProcess` helper at bounded concurrency (`CLASSIFY_CONCURRENCY=4` under the Flash-lite rate ceiling, `STORE_CONCURRENCY=8` under the Supabase pooler). Net: even when the background sync DOES run it finishes in a fraction of the time. **Score-neutral**: nothing in `src/lib/agents/` scoring / DQI / bias / prompts changed; the only behavioral trade is a cold-DB audit gets fewer/no RSS lines in its prompt context — exactly the already-documented non-fatal "proceed with whatever cached data exists" contract; bias detection + DQI never depended on RSS freshness. **Forward-looking rule:** any non-fatal enrichment source on the context-assembly path (news, scholar, macro, industry benchmarks, future ambient sources) MUST be bounded so it can never block the audit; on-demand refresh of such a source is background-only with a small (≤ a few s) wait budget — never a long blocking `await` on the critical path. New sequential per-item I/O in a sync path (LLM batches, DB round-trips) goes through `batchProcess` with a concurrency cap, never a bare `for … await` loop.

- **Friction audit #4 companion — screenshot bugs + mechanized countermeasures (locked 2026-05-17).** The same demo screenshot that surfaced Friction #4 carried two more bugs, both fixed: (1) [WeWorkProofPanel](src/components/marketing/proof/WeWorkProofPanel.tsx) used Next `<Link>` for the static `/dpr-sample-wework.pdf` — `<Link>` RSC-prefetches the href as a route, a static asset has none, so `…pdf?rsc=…` 404'd and console-spammed on /demo (the highest-leverage acquisition surface). Fixed to a plain `<a>`. A whole-class audit confirmed every other static-PDF site (`security`, `how-it-works`, `trust`'s `DownloadCard`, `pricing`) already uses plain `<a>` — WeWorkProofPanel was the lone offender. **Rule: static `public/` assets are always plain `<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">`, NEVER next/link `<Link>`.** (2) [next.config.ts](next.config.ts) CSP had `default-src 'self'` with no `media-src`, so a `data:audio/wav` (almost certainly browser-extension-injected — no first-party `data:audio`/`AudioContext`/`new Audio(` exists in `src/` per exhaustive grep) was blocked AND, more importantly, voice-mode's `<audio>` MediaStream/`blob:` element ([VoiceModePanel.tsx](src/components/founder-hub/voice/VoiceModePanel.tsx)) was silently CSP-degraded. Added `media-src 'self' data: blob:;` — first-party-justified by voice mode, clears the demo console noise. **Mechanized countermeasure** (the "general-scale" answer to "why didn't you catch this"): two new SEMANTIC checks in [audit-platform.mjs](scripts/audit-platform.mjs) — `static-asset-next-link` (any `<Link>` whose href is a static `public/` ext) + `blocking-await-pipeline-path` (a ≥20s `await withTimeout/utilTimeout` in `src/lib/{agents,intelligence,synthesis,copilot}`; the bounded-parallel `Promise.allSettled` fan-out has no leading `await` so it's correctly NOT flagged). Each was proven with a positive test (fires on the real bug shape) AND a negative test (silent on correct code) — a positive-behavior test caught the regex initially used `[wW]ithTimeout`, which would never have matched the actual `utilTimeout` alias the P0 line used (a dead check = false confidence; the exact structure-not-behavior failure that caused the P0, recurring inside its own fix). Both return 0 against the fixed tree (grep-before-assert). Durable discipline lives in memory [feedback-verify-behavior-not-structure](memory) (CRITICAL META rule #8). **Forward-looking rule:** when adding any lint/audit guard, prove it with a positive + negative behavior test, never just "0 findings against the current tree."

- **Friction audit #4 follow-through — post-incident mask/structure sweep (locked 2026-05-17).** After the retrospective, swept the three highest-value residual classes. **(1) Silent-catch dangerous subset — CLEAN.** Audited every `.catch(=>trivial)` in commerce (`stripe`/`billing`), audit-log writers, nudge/email delivery, and the outcome/recalibration/brier flywheel. Zero banned-class swallows: commerce has none; `logAudit` ([audit.ts](src/lib/audit.ts)) `log.error`s + fails-open (correct); the delivery/flywheel hits are all read-for-display (Slack status counts, the founder's internal `metrics/route.ts` `.count().catch(=>0)`) or a read-pref that fails _open toward_ delivery (`email.ts:513`) — the allowed class, no swallowed writes. The fire-and-forget + Stripe-fail-closed locks held. **Residual blind spot (RESOLVED 2026-05-25 — see Silent-catch ratchet trajectory `198 → 199` for the ship):** `scripts/lint-silent-catches.mjs` was single-line only (`lines[i].match`), structurally blind to multi-line `.catch(\n  () => null)` on delivery/audit/flywheel writes — same risk class as the Stripe deal-audit bug that escaped lint and was caught only by manual audit. The 2026-05-25 fix switched the scanner to whole-file matching + line-number derivation; the existing regex already supported multi-line via `\s*` between tokens. The triage feared many existing benign multi-line catches surfacing — in practice only 1 catch was multi-line-only (FK-cascade cleanup in /api/cron/enforce-retention, a legitimate exception now annotated inline), so the baseline bumped 198 → 199 without a sweep. **(2) CLAUDE.md mount-claim doc-masks (generalised C4) — CLEAN.** Verified the 10 highest-value recent `[Component](path) mounted on/renders on/wired into` lock claims against real JSX usage: all 10 have exactly one real mount site matching the claim. The C4 case (DiscoveryGradeImpactCard, 0 mount sites) was an isolated stale-after-refactor claim, already corrected — not systemic. Scope honesty: the load-bearing recent component-mount class was verified, NOT every factual claim in CLAUDE.md. **(3) New mechanized check `sequential-io-loop-pipeline-path`** in [audit-platform.mjs](scripts/audit-platform.mjs) — the unbounded sibling of `blocking-await-pipeline-path`: a `for…of`/`.forEach`/`while` on the audit path whose body `await`s Prisma/LLM/`fetch` (N serial round-trips — the news-sync's 210 serial upserts + 11 serial Gemini batches shape). `Promise.all`/`Promise.allSettled`/`batchProcess` concurrency + `for await (…stream)` consumption are NOT flagged; inline `// audit-allow-sequential` opts out a deliberately-serial loop. Proven with 10 positive+negative behavior assertions (every loop form fires; stream/batchProcess/Promise.all/in-memory/opt-out/sibling-await stay silent); 0 findings vs the tree (the news serial loops were fixed in Friction #4 + live in `src/lib/news/` which is intentionally outside `PIPELINE_PATH`). **Deliberate scoping lock:** do NOT add `news` to `PIPELINE_PATH` — `fetchFeed`'s legitimate 25s `await withTimeout` runs inside `batchProcess(NEWS_FEEDS,…)` (correct bounded-parallel) but the per-line `blocking-await` check can't see the wrapper, so widening scope manufactures a false positive (the noisy-check anti-pattern the codebase explicitly avoids). `PIPELINE_PATH` stays `agents|intelligence|synthesis|copilot` — the orchestration layer where a serial blocking await is unambiguously wrong.

- **Demo redaction-modal + PII-scanner precision + audit-check sharpening (locked 2026-05-17).** Screenshot showed the /demo redaction modal calling "Why Now", "Exit Thesis", "Project Baobab", "Tiger Brands", "Lagos Office" etc. _person names_ (24 garbage hits). **Root cause:** [redaction-scanner.ts](src/lib/utils/redaction-scanner.ts) `NAME_RE` matched ANY two Title-Case words and tried to subtract non-names via a deny-LIST — an unbounded set (project codenames, section headers, deal vocab, company/geo phrases). **Fix (correctness):** inverted to a bounded **common-word/demonym/business-vocab rejection** applied to EITHER token (that set IS enumerable; ~every false bigram contains ≥1) + a positive `HONORIFIC_RE` signal in the ~28 preceding chars that rescues a real name even when a token is common ("Prepared by Dr. Helen Cash"). Precision-over-recall is the file's documented intent (pre-submit safety net with per-hit deselect, not a compliance filter — a wall of garbage trains the user to "Skip redaction"). 16/16 regression tests lock it ([redaction-scanner.test.ts](src/lib/utils/redaction-scanner.test.ts)): the canonical demo memo went ~24 name-hits → ≤2 (only the real name survives); real names + honorific-rescue preserved. **Fix (UX):** [RedactionPreModal](src/components/ui/RedactionPreModal.tsx) footer was a cramped right-bunched 3-button row + a long "Continue without redacting" label overflowing `sm:max-w-lg`. Redesigned: status moved to its own centred line; three actions spread full-width (`flex:1`/`flex:1.4`) with colour-not-size carrying the Cancel/Skip/primary hierarchy; label shortened to "Skip redaction"; the expandable per-hit review list capped at `maxHeight:220` so a long list can't push the footer off-screen. **Legacy-Gemini audit (asked alongside): CLEAN — no action.** Every direct-SDK site is there by deliberate, documented decision: 12-node pipeline + cross-reference + structural-assumptions + outcome-inference + copilot/synthesis + quick-score/human-audit are Phase-3-gated (founder OK + regression plan + held-out before/after DQI sample required — NOT a miss); the grounding family (rpd-simulator/trends/scholarSearch/macroContext — Google-Search grounding the Gateway doesn't expose), `rag/embeddings` (Gemini `TaskType` embeddings Gateway doesn't cover), and `health/route` (must ping the _direct_ key by design) correctly stay; `message-generator`/`profile-extractor`/`founder-context`/`CorePipelineTab` were false hits (model-router import or prose, no SDK call). Nothing has drifted outside the Phase-2 boundary; the only remaining migration is the pipeline, which is the founder-gated Phase 3 — do NOT silently do it. **Audit-check sharpening:** the 4 `dark-mode-tailwind-token` findings were ALL false positives — `text-white`/`bg-white/20` on a `bg-[var(--accent-primary)]` button (correct white-on-colour contrast) + a translucent icon-chip. A cry-wolf check trains the founder to ignore VISUAL (itself a small mask), so `checkDarkModeTokens` in [audit-platform.mjs](scripts/audit-platform.mjs) gained two precise skips (CSS-var/hex-driven coloured background on the same element; the small `w-N h-N rounded bg-white/≤25` icon-chip idiom) — proven with 5 positive+negative behavior assertions; `dark-mode-tailwind-token` 4→0 while real `bg-zinc-900`/`text-gray-400`/full-bleed-overlay violations still flag. The 766 `hardcoded-hex-color` stays the CLAUDE.md-documented low-severity/mostly-intentional backlog (recharts requires hex, severity maps, jsPDF) — explicitly not-blocking; not boiled. **Forward-looking rule:** the PII scanner is precision-first by design — when extending it, add to `COMMON_WORD`/`HONORIFIC_RE` (bounded sets), never reach back for a non-name deny-LIST (unbounded, the bug class). When an audit check produces false positives, tighten it with a precise, behavior-tested skip (or ALLOWED entry) — never let it cry wolf; a noisy check is a mask.

- **Decisions / Decision Rooms / doc-detail layout declutter (locked 2026-05-17).** Three screenshot-reported format problems. **(1) Decisions page over-stacked:** the always-expanded `IntelligentAntagonistPrompt` (~10-row block: eyebrow + h2 + 4-line paragraph + 3-row textarea + footer) dominated above the kanban. Made it **collapsible** — a single slim bar by default (`ShieldQuestion` + "Name your priority first — the antagonist that costs no political capital" + Expand), one click to the full form; expanded block also tightened (padding 20/24→16/18, the dense paragraph trimmed to one sentence). The discipline is preserved (prompt still first; the strip below never pre-empted it anyway) — this is consolidation-not-removal per the "all features stay" rule. **(2) Decision Rooms doubled header + broken empty-state box:** the page wrapper (`decision-rooms/page.tsx`) renders the canonical `.page-header` AND `DecisionRoomsContent` rendered its OWN duplicate `<h1>Decision Rooms</h1>` + "0 rooms total" — the doubled title. Removed the in-content header (now a slim count + Create-Room action row), same content-component-under-a-page-that-owns-chrome discipline as the Decision DNA fold. The "5 30/100 C (55/100)" garbage overlapping the empty-state copy was the **root cause: [IntelligenceBrief](src/components/ui/IntelligenceBrief.tsx) was still 100% Tailwind-classed** (`text-muted` / `bg-secondary/20` / `text-red-400` / `border-border/60`) — the EXACT light-theme-washout drift the EnhancedEmptyState redesign fixed for its sibling primitive (see that file's header). **Root-cause fix: migrated IntelligenceBrief to CSS-var inline styles** (loading skeleton, container, tip, stats row, top-risk-bias chips, `CONTEXT_ICONS` colours) — fixes the broken box on ALL ~8 `showBrief` surfaces, not just Decision Rooms. `dark-mode-tailwind-token` audit count went to 0 (no new tokens introduced). **(3) Doc-detail dead space under the PDF:** the shared `DecisionDetailShell` left `<section>` was a hard `maxHeight: calc(100vh-100px)` + `overflow:hidden` + `sticky` viewport-box; in the 2-col grid the right column (verdict cluster + long R²F tab body) runs much taller, stranding a big empty void below the capped PDF card. Dropped the forced viewport cap → `alignSelf:start`, content-height. **That fixed the OLD void (the capped fixed box) but not the inherent grid mismatch** — a short document beside the much-taller R²F column still left a screen of dead space (the 2026-05-18 founder screenshot). **The fuller fix SHIPPED 2026-05-18 (founder-signed-off, on main):** the left pane is now **sticky-follow** — `position:sticky; top:72; maxHeight:calc(100vh-96px); overflow:auto` — so it pins just below the sticky header and stays beside whatever R²F card you scroll to (no dead space), and a PDF taller than the viewport scrolls INSIDE the pane instead of clipping (the `overflow:hidden`→`auto` change also fixes a latent mobile clip). Safe on the shared shell (documents + deals + packages) WITHOUT a separate verification branch because `DocumentDetailShell.module.css` ALREADY force-overrides `.left` to `position:static !important` + `max-height:70vh/60vh !important` at ≤1100px / ≤640px — the desktop sticky is structurally impossible to apply on mobile/tablet, so the cross-surface blast radius the earlier deferral worried about is neutralised by the existing media queries. The Item-1 above-fold IA lock is in the RIGHT pane — untouched. **Forward-looking rule:** when a primitive renders a "broken/washed-out card" on a light surface, check for un-migrated Tailwind dark utility classes FIRST (the recurring drift class — EnhancedEmptyState, now IntelligenceBrief) and migrate the primitive to CSS-var inline styles (fixes every consumer) rather than hiding it on one page.

- **Tailwind-literal-palette washout — mechanized + canonical-mapping backlog (locked 2026-05-17).** IntelligenceBrief shipped a washed-out box past every gate because the `dark-mode-tailwind-token` check only caught `text-white`/`bg-zinc`/`text-gray-N` — NOT literal palette colours (`text-red-400`, `bg-blue-500`, `text-emerald-400`) which are a FIXED hue ignoring the light-only theme + the CLAUDE.md "use var(--…) / shadcn token, never literal palette" rule. **System fix:** new precise `tailwind-literal-palette` SEMANTIC check in [audit-platform.mjs](scripts/audit-platform.mjs) — regex shape `<prop>-<colour>-<NNN>` CANNOT match the legit shadcn token family (`text-foreground`/`text-muted-foreground`/`bg-muted`/`border-border`/`bg-secondary`/`text-destructive` — no numeric suffix), so it's precise by construction; 12/12 positive+negative behavior assertions; reuses the dark-mode allowlist (viz/marketing/dpr/demo/glass) + dark-severity-card-interior skip + `intentional-dark` file-header opt-out. **Real offender set: 218 findings across 30 files** (NOT the 387 the raw grep falsely inflated — the shadcn token family is legit and correctly excluded). **Canonical migration mapping (deterministic continuation recipe):** `blue|sky|indigo|cyan → var(--info)` · `green|emerald|teal|lime → var(--success)` · `red|rose → var(--error)` · `amber|yellow|orange → var(--warning)` · `purple|violet|fuchsia|pink → var(--accent-secondary)` · neutral greys → `var(--text-muted)`/`var(--text-secondary)`. Chip pattern `bg-X-500/10 text-X-400 border-X-500/20` → `style={{ background:'color-mix(in srgb, var(--Y) 10%, transparent)', color:'var(--Y)', borderColor:'color-mix(in srgb, var(--Y) 25%, transparent)' }}`. **Worked examples (the two contained patterns):** (a) primitive-with-Tailwind-classes → CSS-var inline (IntelligenceBrief, 2026-05-17 — fixed every showBrief surface); (b) config-map-driven (`{label,color:'text-amber-400'}` → `{label,color:'var(--warning)'}` + consumer `className`→`style`): [BiologicalRiskBadge](src/components/ui/BiologicalRiskBadge.tsx) (8→0) + [RelatedDecisions](src/components/ui/RelatedDecisions.tsx) (7→0) migrated as the reference. **Backlog policy (this codebase's established discipline for a large mechanical class — identical to the silent-catch 188 / count-drift 75 ratchets, which both started high and shrink over sessions): the remaining ~203 sites are a MECHANICALLY-TRACKED, CAN-ONLY-SHRINK, DOCUMENTED backlog — `npm run audit:platform` reports the live `tailwind-literal-palette (N)` count; migrate opportunistically by surface priority (wow-moment doc-detail tabs + shared `ui/` primitives first) using the canonical mapping; NEVER introduce a NEW literal-palette class on a platform surface (the check is the enforcement).** This is NOT a dangling thread — it is the codebase's canonical treatment; a 218-blind-edit single churn would be the reckless cut (unverifiable visual regressions + half-migrated files = the actual dangling thread the boil-the-ocean rule forbids). **Deferred subset (flagged, needs care):** the severity-ternary-className logic (`cond ? 'bg-red-500/15 text-red-400 border-red-500/30' : …` in RedTeamTab/OverviewTab/DQChainTab) needs per-component style-object restructuring + a browser pass — higher risk than the contained config-map/icon cases; do these with eyeball verification, not blind. **Forward-looking rule:** when a primitive renders a washed-out card on a light surface, check for literal Tailwind palette FIRST (the recurring drift class — IntelligenceBrief → this lock); migrate the primitive (fixes every consumer) using the canonical mapping; the audit check now catches any NEW occurrence at audit time, not in a screenshot. **Progress (2026-05-18):** session drove the live count 137 → 14 (the 14 residual are the documented allowlisted/false-positive set — GlassMicroInteractions glass-effect + the `founder-context.ts`/`DecisionTriageWidget`/`CalibrationContent` comment-text false positives). Split by risk per the deferred-subset note: **Batch A (3 layout-neutral swaps) shipped to main** (commit `0051d994`, 137→134). **Batch B — the full severity-ternary/config-map/hover doc-detail subset (11 files: NoiseJudge · RegulatoryHorizonWidget · FallacyList · RedTeamView · ForgottenQuestionsTab · DQChainTab · OverviewTab · RedTeamTab · FingerprintContent · StructuralAssumptionsPanel · compare/page) — is on review branch `washout/doc-detail-tabs-2026-05-18`, gates-green (tsc + 5 lints), deliberately NOT pushed to main** because the lock itself says this subset "needs eyeball verification, not blind" and the sandbox has no browser. The founder browser-glances the doc-detail tabs + merges — that satisfies the lock's eyeball requirement via human-in-loop rather than skipping it. config-maps were restructured to typed CSS-var objects; severity-ternary-classNames → conditional inline `style` (hover: branches kept as className since `hover:` can't inline; `hover:` colours migrated to Tailwind arbitrary-value `hover:text-[var(--…)]`); dead Tailwind classes already overridden by an existing inline `style` were simply removed (byte-identical render, zero risk). Link `hover:text-blue-200` lighten was substituted with `hover:underline` (affordance preserved, different mechanism) on the 2 research-insight links — note for the glance. **Progress (2026-06-07) — backlog cleared to 0; two record corrections.** (1) The `washout/doc-detail-tabs-2026-05-18` Batch-B branch was NEVER pushed — it lived only in that session's ephemeral sandbox and was lost when the container was reclaimed (the "commit or push or it's gone" rule made real). - **F1 platform calibration baseline (locked 2026-04-29):** synthetic Brier-scored calibration derived from running our published DQI methodology over the 143-case library with hindsight neutralised. The deck-grade answer to "show me your outcome calibration" before customer outcomes accumulate; primary defense against Cloverpop's data-advantage attack vector (CLAUDE.md External Attack Vectors). **Source of truth**: [src/lib/learning/platform-baseline.ts](src/lib/learning/platform-baseline.ts) `computePlatformCalibrationBaseline()` — caches at module init, deterministic. `computeBrierFairPredictedDqi(c)` mirrors `computeSyntheticDQI` from `dqi.ts` but neutralises evidenceQuality (the one dimension that peeks at outcome) so predictions are made without hindsight; uses canonical `WEIGHTS` and `OUTCOME_TO_ACTUAL` from existing methodology. Honest seed numbers (computed 2026-04-29): **Brier 0.258 (fair band)** over 143 cases, **52% classification accuracy** at the C/D grade boundary, between CIA-analyst (0.23) and motivated-amateur (0.35) bands per Tetlock anchors. Methodology version `2.0.0-seed`. **Bundle-safe snapshot**: [src/lib/learning/platform-baseline-snapshot.ts](src/lib/learning/platform-baseline-snapshot.ts) — ~200B literals for client surfaces that cannot afford the 750KB case-library import (notably the landing-page hero strip). Drift between snapshot and live computation is caught by [platform-baseline-snapshot.test.ts](src/lib/learning/platform-baseline-snapshot.test.ts). **Surfaces wired**: (1) Every customer DPR via [provenance-record-data.ts](src/lib/reports/provenance-record-data.ts) `buildOrgCalibration` — when an org has no closed outcomes, `OrgCalibrationSummary.source = 'platform_seed'` with `platformSeed` block populated; the DPR generator at [decision-provenance-record-generator.ts](src/lib/reports/decision-provenance-record-generator.ts) renders a "Calibration · platform seed baseline" strip on page 1. (2) Public endpoint at [/api/intelligence/calibration-baseline](src/app/api/intelligence/calibration-baseline/route.ts) — `force-static` with `public, max-age=86400, immutable` since the case library is compile-time-static. (3) [BiasGenomeContributionCard](src/components/insights/BiasGenomeContributionCard.tsx) discovery state — `PlatformBaselineCallout` renders the baseline alongside the "Log an outcome" CTA so a cold-start org sees a Tetlock-anchored number, not just an empty card; the contribution endpoint at [/api/intelligence/bias-genome/contribution](src/app/api/intelligence/bias-genome/contribution/route.ts) carries the baseline in every response. (4) [InvestorMetricsTracker](src/components/founder-hub/path-to-100m/data/investor-metrics.ts) — new "Platform Calibration Credibility" metric (rank 17, presentation discipline, status `on_track`) with the seed Brier as `diCurrent` and per-org Brier as the 12-month target. (5) [/bias-genome](<src/app/(marketing)/bias-genome/page.tsx>) hero meta strip — new "Calibration baseline" Pill alongside Named biases / Case studies / Industries. (6) Landing-page [HeroCredibilityStrip](<src/app/(marketing)/page.tsx>) — extended from 4 to 5 items, new `Activity`-icon row reading "Brier 0.258 calibration · 143 audited corporate decisions." **Investor narrative**: today's seed is the contractual answer until customer outcomes accumulate via Outcome Gate enforcement. Per-org Brier replaces the seed once an org has ≥1 closed outcome; convergence target is the Tetlock superforecaster band (≤ 0.13) as the data flywheel matures. **Forward-looking rule**: when `ALL_CASES` or `computeBrierFairPredictedDqi` changes, regenerate the snapshot literals in `platform-baseline-snapshot.ts` and bump `PLATFORM_BASELINE_SNAPSHOT_COMPUTED_AT`; the drift test will catch divergence in CI. CalibrationChip locked-state integration is a deferred follow-up (would require extending `/api/calibration/profile`, scope creep beyond F1).

- **F2 path-to-100m/data.ts split (locked 2026-04-29):** the monolithic [src/components/founder-hub/path-to-100m/data.ts](src/components/founder-hub/path-to-100m/data.ts) (3,554 lines / 228KB) is split into 12 per-consumer sub-modules under [src/components/founder-hub/path-to-100m/data/](src/components/founder-hub/path-to-100m/data/). Bought ~6 months of build-OOM headroom (the 04-29 webpack-OOM had been surfaced as a current-pace risk; per the build-hang triage, splitting heavy data files via dynamic import was the documented next move when `webpackBuildWorker: false` no longer suffices). **Sub-modules** (each owns one consumer's data + types): `strengths-weaknesses.ts` (StrengthsWeaknessesMatrix), `r2f.ts` (R2FDeepDive), `category-pitch.ts` (CategoryAndPitchLibrary), `role-playbooks.ts` (RoleOutreachPlaybooks — 1,441 lines, the heaviest), `killer-responses.ts` (KillerResponsesPlaybook), `investor-metrics.ts` (InvestorMetricsTracker), `failure-modes.ts` (FailureModesWatchtower), `network-nodes.ts` (WarmIntroNetworkMap), `ninety-day-actions.ts` (NinetyDayActionPlan), `notebook-lm-follow-ups.ts` (NotebookLmFollowUpLab), `silent-objections.ts` (MarketRealityCheck), `simplified-funnel.ts` (SimplifiedThirtyDayFunnel). **`data.ts` is now a thin barrel re-exporter** (~110 lines) keeping backwards-compat for any accidental `from './data'` import; `SECTION_COUNTS` lives in the barrel since it composes counts across all 12 modules. Each consumer is updated to import from its specific sub-module (e.g. `from './data/role-playbooks'`) so a NotebookLM synthesis edit on one section doesn't ripple-rebuild the others. **No external imports exist** outside `path-to-100m/` so no other call sites needed updating. **Forward-looking rule**: when adding new path-to-100m sections, create a new file under `data/` (consumer-aligned), import it in the barrel, and update both the consumer-pointer table in `data.ts` header AND the F4 lock above. NEVER pour new data into the barrel directly — it should stay <120 lines forever.

- **Personal Social SSOT — voice + 6 archetypes + composer (locked 2026-05-04 — Content Studio backbone):** [src/lib/data/personal-social-system-prompt.ts](src/lib/data/personal-social-system-prompt.ts) is the canonical voice + archetype + META-rule layer that gets injected into every Content Studio generation request. Source: NotebookLM master KB synthesis (notebook 809f5104, 2026-05-04 query) ranked by ROI for the 1-1-1 wedge motion. Six archetypes shipped: (1) **Billion-Dollar Autopsy** (PE/M&A, channels the 2008-financial-crisis paper); (2) **Room Dynamics / FOMU** (corp dev head, channels the metacognition speech); (3) **Cross-Border Reality Check** (Pan-African fund / GC, weaponises the Lagos edge + 19-framework regulatory map + Dangote DPR); (4) **Retainer Justification Flex** (fractional CSO, channels the financial-literacy initiative); (5) **Naked Business Velocity** (fellow founder, weaponises the 16-yo solo-founder constraint via Jason Cohen's Naked Business principle); (6) **Advice vs Reality** (head of strategic planning, anchors to the ${HISTORICAL_CASE_COUNT}-case reference-class corpus). Composer `buildPersonalSocialSystemPrompt({...})` assembles FOUNDER_CONTEXT + voice anchors (Lagos / 16-yo / Mr. Reiner anonymity rule / financial-literacy / metacognition / 2008-crisis paper) + the empathic-mode-first META rule + protected-revenue framing + banned-vocabulary guard (sourced from `BANNED_VOCABULARY` in [icp.ts](src/lib/constants/icp.ts)) + the picked archetype's structural shape + the "Polite but Brutal Pragmatist" META rule into one system prompt. **Auto-picker** at `pickArchetype(topic)` reads keywords (wework / lehman / ic / committee / africa / nigeria / fractional / shipped / conventional) and routes to the highest-fit archetype; founder can manually override via the new picker UI. **Wired into** [/api/founder-hub/content/route.ts](src/app/api/founder-hub/content/route.ts) (replaces the prior inline systemPrompt that had narrow CSO/M&A audience framing — that contradicted the broad-audience lock); accepts optional `archetypeId` body field; logs the picked archetype on every generation. **UI** ([ContentGenerator.tsx](src/components/founder-hub/content-studio/ContentGenerator.tsx)): "Voice Archetype" picker row above the topic input with Auto-pick + 6 ranked options + a green-tinted detail card surfacing Hook → Middle → CTA shape + AVOID block + persona target so the founder LEARNS the archetype while using it (Content Studio is also a learning surface, not just a generator). **Smoke test** at [personal-social-system-prompt.test.ts](src/lib/data/personal-social-system-prompt.test.ts) — 19 vitest assertions locking composer behavior, keyword routing, banned-vocab presence, voice/META block presence, truncation. **Education Room deck** added: `personal_social_archetypes` deck (8 cards: 6 archetypes + the empathic-mode-first cold-context discipline + the Polite-but-Brutal Pragmatist META rule) so the founder can drill the patterns himself before writing without AI assist. **Sister-route audit also shipped**: [WeeklyBrief route](src/app/api/founder-hub/content/weekly-brief/route.ts) had a stale "20-bias taxonomy" string (count drift; 22 now) — fixed to derive from `BIAS_EDUCATION` length; both WeeklyBrief and [ContentOpportunities](src/app/api/founder-hub/content/opportunities/route.ts) had narrow CSO/M&A audience copy contradicting the broad-audience lock — broadened to name CSO + M&A + corp dev + fund partner + fractional CSO + head of strategic planning + GC explicitly, and added the empathic-mode-first rule to the brief generation instructions so the briefs flowing back into the drafter are pre-aligned with the SSOT. **Forward-looking rule**: when CLAUDE.md positioning vocabulary changes, edit `icp.ts` only — the personal-social SSOT inherits via import. When a new NotebookLM ranked archetype set lands, update `POST_ARCHETYPES` in `personal-social-system-prompt.ts` AND mirror the cards in `education-room-data.ts personal_social_archetypes` deck in the same commit. Never let a new archetype ship without the matching flashcard.

- **Discovery + tailored-pitch hybrid toolkit (locked 2026-05-01 — v3.3 §7 ship):** the most-load-bearing pre-event reference for the next 90 days of in-person events + warm-intro conversations. Three artefacts ship together: (a) [src/lib/data/discovery-pitch-toolkit.ts](src/lib/data/discovery-pitch-toolkit.ts) — typed source-of-truth exporting `DISCOVERY_QUESTIONS` (4 verbatim Mom-Test questions with watch-for cues), `DEFLECTION_SCRIPT` ("I'm researching whether a problem in strategic decision-making is real..."), `PERSONA_OPENERS` (4: cso / ma_corpdev / fund_partner / gc_compliance — fund_partner carries the never-name-Sankore discipline note), `PITCH_TRIGGERS` (8 if-revealed-X-then-pitch-Y triggers covering four-tool-graveyard / specific-blind-spot / audit-committee-Q&A / cross-border-regulatory / never-paid / paying-Cloverpop / AI-assisted-memos / agent-generated-memos), `DISCOVERY_DISCIPLINE_RULES`, `FOLLOWUP_EMAIL_TEMPLATE`, `WHAT_30_CONVERSATIONS_PRODUCE`. (b) [DiscoveryPitchPanel](src/components/founder-hub/sales/DiscoveryPitchPanel.tsx) — interactive component mounted at the TOP of [SalesToolkitTab](src/components/founder-hub/SalesToolkitTab.tsx) (highest visibility); collapsible pitch-trigger cards keyed off discovery signals; persona toggle. (c) [docs/discovery-card-v1.md](docs/discovery-card-v1.md) — printable phone-readable Markdown reference for back-of-Uber pre-event recall. **Why hybrid not pure Mom Test**: founder's burn-rate constraint forces the trade. Pure 30-conversation discovery discipline maximises data quality but burns runway; hybrid preserves data quality (discovery FIRST within each conversation, before any pitch — all 4 Qs in order) while capturing conversion (after Q4, pivot with "Based on what you said about [their pain in their words], I think I have something you should see" + pitch tailored to the signal). Cost: ~10% data-quality erosion as early-conversation pitches anchor framing. Benefit: revenue compounds while discovery accumulates. **Forward-looking rule**: edit the typed exports in `discovery-pitch-toolkit.ts` only; the panel + the Markdown card both regenerate from it. Pattern-match across 10+ conversations before declaring the hybrid working; if the pattern doesn't converge on a coherent 5-word pain language + price band, the wedge is wrong, not the questions.

The migration is in `prisma/migrations/`; founder runs `npx prisma migrate deploy` against production manually per CLAUDE.md "Modifying the analysis pipeline" rule. **Forward-looking rule**: when fixing a Prisma field name typo, always (1) write the migration as RENAME COLUMN (preserves data), (2) verify single sed pattern handles all CamelCase variants, (3) regenerate Prisma client (`npx prisma generate`) and run `tsc --noEmit` BEFORE committing — the type system catches any missed callers loudly.
